顧馨一　談救濟麵粉原則確定　治標：實財鐵交四部負責解决　治本：官商合作力謀麥質改良

Central News Agency reports, regarding the matter of relieving flour, after the efforts of the government authorities and flour manufacturers, the important principles of various reliefs have been determined. Since the United States, known for its wheat production, has encountered a famine this year and its output has decreased, all parties are now seeking to salvage the situation. According to Gu Xinyi, a flour magnate in this city, the following are the details:

Treating the Symptoms and Addressing the Root Cause Simultaneously

According to Gu, I went to the capital earlier and exchanged views with the relevant authorities on the relief of flour. It has now been decided that this matter will be approached from both treating the symptoms and addressing the root cause. In terms of treating the symptoms, efforts will be made to reduce taxes and fees on transportation. The Ministry of Industry will consult with the Ministries of Finance, Railways, and Communications on this matter and be responsible for seeking a solution. At this finance meeting, it was agreed that the consolidated tax should be treated equally. Therefore, the flour consolidated tax should be taxed according to the grades of other goods. First and second-class flours will be taxed according to their grades, while third and fourth-class flours will be exempted from tax. If this can be done, the cost may be reduced. As for addressing the root cause, efforts will be made to improve the quality of wheat. In various wheat-producing areas, mud and sand are often mixed in to increase the weight. Such a trick must be fundamentally improved. The above matters will be improved by local governments and grain merchants.

The American Wheat Famine May Raise Prices

The biggest reason for the slump in the flour market is the oversupply. The reason for the oversupply is the dumping of foreign wheat in the country. In recent years, the import of American wheat has been alarmingly high, causing domestic wheat sales to stagnate. It is now reported that the American wheat-producing region has suffered a disaster, and its output has been greatly reduced, less than half of what it was in previous years. Therefore, it is expected that the American wheat market may increase prices. If so, American wheat may stop being transported to China. If American wheat no longer comes to China, and domestic wheat can be relieved of tax and freight burdens, the flour business will have a chance to recover. The reporter then asked whether the recent strikes in the United States, which have caused the suspension of the shipment of wheat flour borrowed from the United States, have any impact on China's wheat flour market. The answer was that the reason why China's flour manufacturers are in today's depression is largely due to the import of American flour. However, at that time, what China negotiated with the American authorities was only wheat. The matter of flour was not mentioned at first. Later, because American flour manufacturers generally felt a lack of raw materials because the government only exported wheat, and the workers of general flour mills might lose their jobs as a result, they requested the government to allocate flour loans. After several negotiations, it was reduced to 40%. As for the American suspension of transportation due to strikes, it is only a temporary matter. We cannot be optimistic about it. However, since the United States is affected by the wheat famine, if it can stop the shipment of wheat flour to China, China's wheat flour market will have a turnaround. However, since the Northeast was seized by the Japanese, because that place was originally the largest market for the sale of flour in China, although a very small number of flour is now transported there for sale, everything is controlled by the Japanese. This is the fatal injury to China's flour industry.

No News of Guangdong's Agricultural Tax Collection

The reporter further inquired about the report that Guangdong will start collecting agricultural tax on the 16th of this month, so there have been large transactions of grain by the Guangdong merchants in Shanghai. Gu said that he had not heard of this matter, but the Guangdong provincial authorities had collected a fertilizer tax. This tax was originally used to transfer the construction funds of Sun Yat-sen University in Guangdong. As a result, a large number of bean cakes transported from this city were detained in Guangdong due to tax issues. After repeated proofs from various parties, Chen Jitang also asked Yang Dezhao, a representative, to telegraph for relief. The merchants also telegraphed Zou Lu, the president of Sun Yat-sen University, to consider the difficulties of the merchants. The Guangdong provincial authorities agreed to exempt all fertilizer taxes on domestically produced bean cakes entering Guangdong. As for the reported agricultural tax, it may have been a misrepresentation of this matter. Recently, there have been no so-called large transactions of grains in the grain market. Everything is the same as usual.

市商會電中政會　請免芝麻出口稅　體察商情准其减免

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Central Political Council yesterday, saying, "The Nanjing Central Political Council: On the 8th of this month, we received a letter from the Association of the Grain, Oil, and Cake Industry, stating that according to letters from the Grain Merchants and Yuantang, on May 26th, it was reported that the Executive Yuan had passed the principle of reducing export tax rates on domestic goods, and it was said that it had been submitted to the Central Political Council for deliberation," etc. It can be seen that the government's intention to encourage the export of domestic goods and develop international trade is realized. The so-called revitalization of rural areas and relief of industry and commerce will be visible here. Sesame is a major local product in Lu, Yu, Wan, Su, Xiang, and E provinces. Domestic demand is actually small, and exports have always been the main business. Shanghai's exports, at their peak, were about 50,000 tons per year, and they had long occupied a position in international trade. Down to today, it has plummeted, and the export volume is less than one-tenth, which has a significant impact on the rural economy. This time, the Executive Yuan passed the reduction of export tax rates on domestic goods, and sesame is a major export local product, which is expected to be included in the comprehensive collection. However, for the sake of preparation, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce is requested to quickly telegraph the Central Political Council to consider the principle of export tax rates on domestic goods, and to give priority to the reduction of sesame export tax, etc. Based on this, it should be prepared and forwarded, and it is hoped that it will be approved as requested, which is really a public friendship, etc." It is found that this matter was previously on April 29, by the Association to request that the export and transit taxes on raw peanuts and raw sesame oil be completely exempted. After the affiliated association telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, it was approved by the Ministry that the tax rates on peanut kernels and peanut oil would each be reduced by six-tenths for those transported overseas within three months, from May 26 to August 25 of this year. The sesame item was not discussed for reduction. Now, it is claimed that sesame exports were about 50,000 tons per year at their peak, and the current sales are less than one-tenth. After verifying the situation, it is really necessary to reduce and exempt export taxes and provide assistance. It is fortunate that the reduction of export tariffs is under consideration by the council, and the business situation cannot be understood and considered comprehensively. It is urgent to telegraph for approval, and it is hoped that the export tax on sesame will also be included in the reduction and exemption, and handed over to the competent departments for handling separately, which is really for the public convenience. The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce."

拒毒會　發表浙省禁烟成績

The China National Anti-Drug Association received a report from the Zhejiang Provincial Anti-Drug Association on the achievements of drug prohibition in Zhejiang Province, which was quite detailed. The association believed that since Lu Diping took charge of Zhejiang's administration, the ban on opium in Zhejiang Province has been strictly implemented, with remarkable results. Since the convening of the Zhejiang Provincial Anti-Opium Conference in August 1932, which resulted in an anti-opium program, the Zhejiang Provincial Government and the Department of Civil Affairs have been able to implement it according to the proposal, and have dispatched anti-opium commissioners to various districts to investigate and eradicate it, so the harm of opium has been greatly reduced compared to before. Therefore, the investigation report is factual and is specially published as follows:

"Zhejiang Province from October 1932 to September 1933"

8,858 male offenders, 1,315 female offenders

5,527 opium offenders, 4,646 red pill and morphine offenders, etc.

328 fined, 6,945 sentenced to imprisonment

Statistics of anti-opium achievements within the year: total fines of 171,147 yuan, execution of opium offenders: a total of 19 by the Security Department after the promulgation of the Zhejiang Provincial Anti-Opium Program, and a total of 11 by judicial judgment. Anti-opium institutions: established after the promulgation of the Zhejiang Provincial Anti-Opium Program, totaling 59 anti-opium centers, 31 anti-opium hospitals, 52 anti-opium associations, 20 anti-opium branches, and 20 anti-opium sub-branches in Zhejiang Province, totaling 182. Opium factories: a total of 9 currently established. Civilian vocational training centers anti-opium department 8. It is found that Jiutai, Wencu, and other prefectures in Zhejiang have the most opium cultivation, followed by Yongkang in the entire prefecture and Chun'an in Yan prefecture, etc., which have also produced opium. It is estimated that there are about one million mu of opium fields in Zhejiang. After Lu Bicheng, the director of the Department of Civil Affairs, inspected and strictly ordered the anti-opium commissioners to investigate and supervise the eradication, almost all of them have been cleared in the past two years."

地方法院昨焚燬毒物

The Procuratorate of the Shanghai Local Court burned opium, red pills, morphine, narcotics, and smoking paraphernalia confiscated from January to March of this year at 2:00 PM yesterday. The items included 174 taels and 1 mace of opium, 14,458 red pills, 2,564 taels, 20 catties, 63 taels, 2 mace, and 7 fen of morphine, 9 catties and 6 taels of poisonous powder, 589 opium bubbles, 5 taels and 2 mace, and 3,537 pieces of smoking paraphernalia. The destruction was reported to the superiors and burned in public. The personnel who came to supervise the destruction yesterday included Yu Hao from the Jiangsu High Procuratorate, Deng Hui from the Command Headquarters, Huang Chen from the Municipal Government, Ren Bin from the Municipal Party Department, Lu Zonghan from the Jianghai Customs, Chen Mingsheng from the Public Security Bureau, Zhu Fuzeng from the County Government, Xue Shenzhen from the County Public Security Bureau, Xiang Zhejun and Ju Zhijing from the First Special Court, and Gao Yanmao and Zhao Yifen from the Second Special Court. After being greeted by President Shen and Chief Prosecutor Lou, they ordered Police Chief Chen Junfang and Police Sergeants Chen Xihui and Gu Hanqing to supervise the entire body of legal police and servants to stack the narcotics with pine firewood, pour oil and salt, and set them on fire. The burning was completed at 4:00 PM, and the ashes were thrown into the Huangpu River by the servants to remove the toxic substances.

Inland River Steamer Association Petitions for Abolition of Harsh Cargo Barge Taxes

Cargo barges used by inland river small steamers have already paid fees and obtained licenses according to ministerial orders and have also been paying monthly donations to the Municipal Bureau of Finance. However, since June 1st, the customs office has also required the payment of tonnage taxes when cargo is cleared on these barges. This means that cargo barges in the same location are suddenly burdened with double taxation. This is not only unbearable for shipping merchants but also creates a conflict between central and local government policies. Now, as the government is in the process of abolishing harsh taxes and miscellaneous levies, all cargo barges are demanding the swift cancellation of this illegal overcharging of ship taxes. The Inland River Steamer Association of the city has yesterday submitted a petition to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Transportation, requesting the prompt removal of these harsh taxes.

Through Routes Continue to Reduce Less-than-Carload Freight Rates, Effective July 1st

The Ministry of Railways previously issued instructions to all routes, stipulating that less-than-carload freight rates should be 30% higher than carload freight rates. However, at that time, the Beijing-Shanghai Railway under the jurisdiction of the two railway bureaus charged 100% more, and the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway also charged 75% more. After discussion with the relevant departments, it was uniformly changed to 50% more, and the Ministry of Railways approved it with Directive No. 5326, effective from June 1st, 1933. Recently, it was proposed to further reduce it to 30% more, and the Ministry of Railways has approved it, effective from July 1st.

Consecration Ceremony of the Chinese Holy Anglican Church Bishop of Shaanxi

At 10:00 AM today (June 10th), the consecration ceremony of President Shen Zigao as the first Bishop of the Shaanxi Diocese will be held at the All Saints' Church on Route Lafayette in the French Concession. The ceremony will be presided over by Bishop Ouyang Zhi of Beiping, Dean of the House of Bishops, and assisted by bishops from various provinces. The ceremony is solemn and marks a new era for the domestic missionary dioceses of the Chinese Holy Anglican Church and is truly a bright and brilliant page in the history of the Chinese Church. All Saints' Church, in view of the inevitable congestion of those going to the church to pay their respects on this day, has specially printed complimentary tickets and distributed them to fellow believers in various churches, and it is said that they have been exhausted. After the ceremony, the eleven Shanghai Anglican Churches will jointly host a public banquet for the new bishop, bishops from various provinces, and representatives at the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA. In the afternoon at 4:00 PM, there will be a welcome tea party at the New Asia Hotel on North Sichuan Road, which all believers from various churches are welcome to attend. According to reports, Bishop Shen Zigao is a Bachelor of Arts and Bachelor of Divinity from St. John's University in Shanghai. He presided over the Daosheng Church in Xiaguan, Nanjing, for seventeen years. In 1929, he went to Europe and the United States to study various church affairs and entered Oxford and Cambridge Universities in England to study theology for two years. He has served as Chairman of the House of Representatives of the General Synod of the Chinese Holy Anglican Church. At the current National General Synod of the Chinese Holy Anglican Church, the House of Bishops and the House of Representatives unanimously elected him as the first Bishop of Shaanxi, which can be said to be a great gain for the church and the Northwest.

Nanshi Rent Reduction Association Submits Petition to the Executive Yuan, Requesting Approval of Property Valuation to Begin Rent Reduction

The Nanshi District Rent Reduction Association of Shanghai, located in Yongqing Lane on Minquan Road, is a group of rent reduction branches in the entire Nanshi district. Since the rent reduction movement began, more than 80 branches have been established. Using stern words and justice, they advised landlords to moderately reduce rent. Fearing that some people would use the name of rent reduction to default on rent, they specifically published a statement stating that branches that have not registered with the association will not be involved. They are now actively working to seek liberation for the public. Yesterday, they submitted a petition to the Executive Yuan for approval. The original text is recorded below: "Presenting a petition for rents that are too high, hindering livelihoods, and should be reduced to relieve the suffering of the people. Humbly requesting review and approval and submission to the Executive Yuan meeting for special discussion and implementation. Since the January 28th Incident, Shanghai has suffered a great loss of vitality, and the market is in a slump. Those who are imprisoned for debt and the unemployed who become beggars are everywhere. Other problems include the difficulty in selling goods, financial stagnation, hopelessness of prosperity, and the danger of bankruptcy. Therefore, the masses have risen up to demand rent reduction to relieve the suffering of the people. However, most landlords hold the law as a protective talisman, and lawsuits fill the courts, causing complaints and resentment. They use the name of rent arrears to oppress the actual situation, resulting in seeking peace but feeling uneasy, and increasing litigation burdens before rent is reduced. People's minds are restless, as if a great disaster is imminent. The association is a group to reduce rents and cannot sit idly by and watch the city turn into ruins and the people become starving. However, to break through the difficulties, we should first seek a way out. Reducing rents is the only way to alleviate the emergency. Low rents mean lighter burdens, and lighter burdens mean the people's suffering is relieved. Once the people's suffering is relieved, the market can prosper, and the market can prosper, then vitality can be restored. Therefore, we have specifically collected public opinions and formulated measures, based on the Shanghai land price promulgated by the Shanghai Land Bureau this year as a benchmark, to calculate the land price, plus construction costs, so that we know the cost of the house and set the rental rate to ensure fairness. Therefore, we start organizing the Shanghai Rent Reduction Evaluation Committee, submit it to the Municipal Party Department and the Social Affairs Bureau for supervision and evaluation, and submit it to the Land Bureau to prove the land price, and hire Shanghai famous architects and carpentry trade unions to estimate the construction cost, so that we can understand the cost of the house and determine the rental rate. Only by adopting a compromise method can we maintain fairness, and then all disputes between landlords and tenants can be easily resolved. According to this method, landlords have considerable profits to gain, and tenants have no excessive rent burden, so we can coexist and prosper together to seek the development of the market. Therefore, we investigate and consider all requests for rent reduction in detail and impartially to seek mutual understanding between the two parties. However, the tongue is scorched and the lips are worn out, but it is difficult to return to the landlord's hearing. The pen is withered and the ink is exhausted, and it is not allowed to reduce it by a cent. However, rent reduction in the capital has already been implemented. What crime has Shanghai committed that it is still in dire straits? You are a veteran of the party and the country and a lucky star for the people. I dare to ask for your compassionate heart that is already hungry and drowned, and to issue a grand decree that includes the people and all things. Please consider the economic downturn and high rents in Shanghai and approve the proposal to reduce rents so that prosperity can be expected, the Republic of China can be revived, the Communist Party will have fewer opportunities to confuse and incite, and the citizens will have more hope of recovery. All the reasons for rent reduction, in addition to submitting a petition to the Shanghai Municipal Government, the Municipal Council, and various organizations, we hereby submit this document for your review and implementation. We cannot help but wait for your order with apprehension. Respectfully submitted to President Wang of the Executive Yuan."

At around 10:00 AM, Prosecutor Zhang Junqing, appointed by the First Special District District Court, accompanied Forensic Doctor Zhang Yan, Clerk Wang Zuyi, and others to the office to examine the body, ascended the public case, and inquired about the case. The deceased was indeed her younger brother, named Changxi, 28 years old, who had been working as a temporary clerk in the Second Special Court for several years. He suddenly suffered from mental illness several years ago, and it came and went. She still has a father, who is now in Beiping. On the 2nd of this month, her second uncle came to Shanghai from Beiping and said that his father was very sick. When her younger brother heard about it, his old illness relapsed. Unexpectedly, he went out on a trip and committed suicide in a hotel. She now asks to be allowed to claim the body. Zhang agreed to the statement and ordered that the deceased, Ouyang Rixi, male, was indeed found to have died of poisoning before his death. Municipal Federation of Trade Unions Petitions for Ban on Prize Savings, Money Flows Out of the Country, No Different from Aiding the Enemy with Money, Deeply Hope that the Central Government Will Take Decisive Action to Express the National Economy

The Shanghai Municipal Federation of Trade Unions believes that prize savings exploit the blood and sweat of the people, and specifically presents it to the Municipal Party Department, requesting it to forward it to the Central Party Department, the National Government, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and other agencies. The original text reads, "Presenting a petition for the proposal by Ma Yinchu and ten others at the National Financial Conference to strictly prohibit the prize savings of the Universal and Sino-French Savings Associations. It is far-sighted and the evils are clear. All those who are concerned about the people's livelihood express their sympathy. We now humbly present the reasons, begging you to take decisive action as soon as possible,

Prohibit Immediately

to eliminate social hidden dangers and maintain the national economy. We humbly believe that the establishment of the two savings associations began in the era of the Beijing government. At that time, their power was very weak, and the government was also ignorant and did not pay attention to it. Later, their power gradually expanded, and people in society paid a little attention to it. However, at that time, the savings funds were only 20 to 30 million. Recently, their power has increased day by day, and the savings funds have increased to 80 to 90 million. Just take

Universal One Family

as an example, the total number of depositors has exceeded 130,000. The total amount of depositors is the whole association, and its monthly savings revenue reaches 1.6 million. On an annual basis, it is no less than 20 million, and the Sino-French association is not included. Why are these huge sums of money not the blood and sweat of our people? However, we allow foreign businessmen to manipulate and control them. Our government has no opportunity to supervise and intervene. If an accident occurs, the blood and sweat of these 80 to 90 million Chinese people will all be turned into nothing. We still remember the case of the Oriental Bank Savings Company

Defrauded Huge Amounts of Money

The blood and sweat of the Chinese people were all taken away. Moreover, its savings nature is no different from today's Universal and Sino-French. The overturned cart can be a warning, how can we not be terrified? This is one. Moreover, savings is a virtue and is also a way to promote national thrift. Collaboration of Local Bullies and Police Chief; Secret Red Pill Manufacturing Operation; Gross Illegalities by Public Servants; To Be Handed Over to Military Authorities for Interrogation

Within a week, Director Wen Hong'en of the Municipal Police Bureau received as many as seven anonymous reports, roughly stating that Liu Zhizhen, a local bully from Hebei in Zhabei, had colluded with Yuan Fuchen and Wang Futian, police chiefs of the First Precinct of the Fifth District, and others, a few months ago. They had set up a large-scale red pill manufacturing operation on the overpass at No. 111, Delin Xili, Baoxing East Road, within the jurisdiction of the precinct. They hired many workers to rush production day and night, transporting the pills to various places for sale, engaging in both wholesale and retail of loose pills and lamp-smoking paraphernalia. Director Wen was greatly shocked upon receiving the report, as he was mindful of the strict prohibition of highly addictive drugs recently promulgated by Chairman Chiang of the Nanchang Headquarters Military Affairs Commission.

He felt compelled to thoroughly investigate and arrest those involved. He secretly ordered Detective Captain Lu Ying to dispatch a large number of detectives to rush to the address for a surprise arrest on the evening before last around 6:00 PM. As a result, Liu Zhizhen (39 years old), a woman named Liu Lin (45 years old), Yuan Fuchen (28 years old, from Hebei), police chief of the First Precinct of the Fifth District, Wang Futian (45 years old), petition police Shang Zhenjiang (38 years old), and Ni Bin (39 years old, from Zhejiang), and other six persons were apprehended on the spot. A red pill gun, a smoking lamp, and dozens of red pills were confiscated. They were immediately taken directly to the bureau. The next day, Director Wen summoned Chief Bao of the precinct to the bureau for a stern interrogation, but he swore to deny any knowledge of the matter. However, Director Wen, considering the gravity of the matter in relation to the prohibition order from superiors, and intending to punish one as a warning to a hundred, decided to transfer the case to the military authorities for strict handling after further interrogation, in accordance with the latest regulations prohibiting highly addictive drugs.

Hongqiao Sanatorium to Be Completed Soon; Mayor Wu and Others Enthusiastically Support It

Mr. Ding Fubao of Xishan spent decades translating Eastern and Western medical classics, amounting to hundreds of works, advocating for the reform of medicine, and his contributions were immense. In recent years, he retired to Shanghai, focusing on literature and diligently studying ancient texts. His Buddhist Dictionary and Shuowen Jiezi Gulin Zhenxu Bian were successively published and have been recognized as extremely valuable works in academic circles. Last year marked the sixtieth birthdays of Mr. Ding and his wife, Madam Wang. His son, Dr. Hui Kang, and others, wanted to hold a birthday celebration. However, Mr. Ding, considering the difficulties of the times, strongly opposed extravagance. Furthermore, recognizing the lack of sanatoriums close to nature in the densely populated and bustling city of Shanghai, he chose a quiet and open area on Hongqiao Road in Western Shanghai to build a state-of-the-art sanatorium to serve the needs of the community and leave behind a lasting memento. Since construction began, the project has taken more than a year due to its vast scale. It is now reported that the interior construction will be completed within the month. Mr. Ding has no particular hobbies in life, and this magnificent building, which will soon meet us, is entirely thanks to his daily thrift and frugality. His dedication to social welfare, growing stronger with age, is deeply admirable.

General Outline of the Construction: The designer of the sanatorium is Dr. Xi Fuquan, an engineering doctor from Qiming Architectural Company, and the contractor is An Ji Construction Company. The entire sanatorium ensures ample intake of light and air, and special attention has been paid to soundproofing and fire prevention. The buildings are all constructed with steel and reinforced concrete. A special feature is that all bedrooms face south, and each room has a separate balcony and hot and cold water pipes. In addition to various medical rooms, there are also facilities such as a social hall, dining room, library, music room, and sunbathing platform.

General Equipment: The operating room, dining room, and special-class rooms of the sanatorium are equipped with cold air systems in addition to heating pipes. The lighting in the operating room adopts the latest shadowless method. The X-ray machine has anti-vibration devices and is one of the most modern types. In addition, short-wave diathermy machines, sun lamps capable of irradiating sixteen people's entire bodies, and ultraviolet glass windows are used in bathrooms and special wards. All bedroom furnishings are made of stainless steel for ease of disinfection. In addition to hiring specialized physicians in chemistry and X-rays and experienced Chinese and Western nurses, the medical services will be entirely directed by prominent doctors in Shanghai.

Support from All Sectors: Mr. Ding's old friends, such as Yu Youren, Wu Zhihui, Dai Chuanxian, Ye Chucang, Gu Mengyu, and others, are all initiators of the sanatorium. In addition, President Wang, President Sun, Mayor Wu, Secretary-General Yu, Director Wen, Director Shen, former Mayor Zhang Dingfan, Zheng Hongnian, Du Yuesheng, and others have enthusiastically supported it, serving as initiators and donating various valuable medical equipment.

Bao Shan Seawall to Be Repaired

The Jiangsu Provincial Government has resolved to allocate 400,000 yuan to repair the seawalls of the three counties of Bao, Tai, and Song, and construction has now begun. A general office has been set up within the Baoshan Seawall Engineering Bureau, with Peng Yumo as the general director and Gu Houxi as the director of the Baoshan section. It has since been learned that the most critical sections of the Baoshan area, including Gu Longdun, Zhangjiazhai, Zhutoujing, and Beishidong, total 540 gongzhang [approximately 540 meters] in length and require 300,000 yuan, exceeding the provincial government's allocated 200,000 yuan by approximately 100,000 yuan. It is reported that the amount of money required for the Songjiang and Taicang counties is less than 100,000 yuan. The deadline for completion of each section is five months, and Shen Baixian, the head of the Jiangsu Construction Department, is scheduled to personally inspect the progress once a week.

French Police Attach Importance To the Assassination Case on Rue Say Zoong; Ordered Reactionary Criminals to Identify Whether the Two Corpses Were Old Friends; After Opening the Coffins for Inspection, All Claimed Not to Know the Deceased

Chen Fangruo, a native of Hubei, residing in the garret of a three-story building at No. 64, Shanfu Li, Lane 148, Rue Say Zoong in the French Concession, and his wife, Liu Jie, were suddenly assassinated at their home by two thugs carrying two baskets of loquats on the morning of the 8th around 8:00 AM, on the pretext of delivering gifts. Both husband and wife were shot in vital organs and died instantly. After receiving the report, the French police dispatched detectives to investigate the murderers separately. They also transported the bodies to the Tongren Fuyuan mortuary for examination. The Second Special Court was notified on the same day to send personnel to confirm the cause of death. As there were no family members, the mortuary took care of the coffining and burial of the bodies. The details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. As ordered, the Tongren Fuyuan mortuary coffined the two corpses that night and instructed carriers to transport them to the Nanshi Salvation Bureau in the early morning yesterday for shipment to the Tangwan cemetery in Pudong for burial. However, the police attached great importance to this case, fearing that the deceased were related to political reactionaries. Therefore, yesterday morning, they notified the Tongren Fuyuan mortuary to instruct the Salvation Bureau to send a small steamer to follow and intercept the coffins halfway, hoisting the two coffins back to the mortuary. Subsequently, the Political Department of the French Police transferred three reactionary criminals, Tong Shiduo, Liu Zhaoshan, and Chen Cihang, who had been arrested and sentenced by the Jiangsu High Court Third Branch Court and were detained in the detention center during the appeal period, to the police station. Detectives were dispatched to take them to the mortuary to identify whether they knew the deceased. After a thorough and detailed inspection, all claimed not to know the deceased. Tong and others were then sent back to the High Court Third Branch Court for detention. However, the police originally planned to move the two corpses to the refrigerated room of the mortuary attached to the Shanghai Municipal Council Hospital on Route Tenant de la Tour, preparing for a re-examination on Monday. Subsequently, it was decided not to proceed with this inspection procedure, and the Tongren Fuyuan mortuary was notified to collect the two corpses again and transport them to the cemetery for burial.

Three Kidnappers Executed by Firing Squad; Before Execution, They Complained about the Hardships of General Prisoners; Not Enough Food and Frequent Abuse

Ma Gensheng, a local kidnapper, 41 years old, Guan Afu from Yangzhou, 31 years old, and Ren Zixiang from Shaoxing, 39 years old, were charged with using weapons to conspire with accomplices to kidnap Madam Yang Ren on South Chengdu Road and Weihaiwei Road around 9:00 PM on October 24 of the 19th year of the Republic of China [1930]. On the afternoon of November 2 of the 11th year [1932], they kidnapped Sheng Yishao at No. 32 Shandong Road. On the morning of December 9 of the same year, they kidnapped Le Zhenbao near Yu Yuan Road and Hart Road. Le was the owner of Taichang Wood Shop on Nanjing Road. They hid their hostage at No. 911 Haig Road and demanded a huge ransom. After the case was uncovered, the Old Zhabei Police arrested them and transferred them to the First Special District Court. After interrogation, they were all sentenced to death, and the sentence was approved by the Jiangsu Provincial Government. Yesterday morning, the execution date arrived. The police transferred the three criminals, Ma, etc., to the Third Criminal Court. Judge Shen Shanzeng presided over the session, and Mr. Li Zhishan, a lawyer from the Shanghai Municipal Council, presented the case files, photos, etc., for inspection. The court asked the three criminals if they had any last words and sent letters to their families. Ma Gensheng confessed that he used to run a hardware store and had an elderly mother, wife, and daughters at home. He requested that his brother, Ma Jinfa, collect his body from the execution ground. Guan Afu confessed that he used to be a chauffeur and currently had two older sisters in the courtroom. He requested permission to say a few words. The court granted his request, and he told his sisters not to cry, entrusting them with important family matters and asking them to collect his body. Ren Zixiang confessed that he used to work at a money exchange. His family had known about his death sentence for a long time. He had a friend named Lu Jigeng who embezzled 100 yuan in introduction fees for a tea waiter's deposit box. He asked his wife, Zhu, to pursue the matter. He also mentioned that he owned some houses and land in his hometown, which should be managed by her. The three criminals all maintained a calm demeanor, stating that they should obey the law and die for their crimes of kidnapping. However, they complained that they were not given enough to eat in prison every day, suffering from hunger. There were also cases of inmates starving to death because they were not given food for various reasons. They also stated that two Westerners, Numbers 37 and 2, often beat the prisoners from time to time. They requested that the court find a way to provide relief to the prisoners through the Chinese government. Judge Shen instructed that Ma, Guan, and Ren be sent to the Shanghai District Court Prosecutor's Office for execution by firing squad, escorted by Chinese and Western police officers, along with case files, photos, etc., in a car to the Caojing Second Prison execution ground. After the prosecutor verified the identities of the three criminals, Ma, etc., he ordered the judicial police to tie them up according to law and carry out the execution by firing squad.

The home of Shen Guixing, a local resident residing at No. 35 Sande Li, Panjiawan, Zhabei, caught fire around 7:00 PM the night before last, caused by a cigarette butt that fell into a pile of straw. Chen Qing, Inspector of the Municipal Police Bureau, Suddenly Attacked Last Night; Police Officer on Duty Shot and Wounded by Thugs' Accomplices; Chen Shot in the Chest, Condition Very Critical

Chen Qing, a native of Danyang, 25 years old, an inspector in the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau, went to the Hou Defu Restaurant on Guangxi Road last night around 8:00 PM for dinner at the invitation of a friend. Chen was dressed in a light-colored suit and behaved very elegantly. It was not until around 10:00 PM that the dinner ended and they dispersed. Chen and his friend went downstairs together, and each parted ways when they reached the entrance of the restaurant. Chen walked alone along Guangxi Road towards Nanjing Road. Unexpectedly, a thug wearing short clothes suddenly rushed from across the street. Seeing this, Chen knew something was wrong and quickly ran away. However, the thug already had a gun in his hand. Seeing Chen running away, he fired two shots at him, one of which hit him in the chest. Chen continued to run forward in pain, crossing Hankou Road, about ten yards, before collapsing to the ground, bleeding profusely. At that time, the Chinese police officer on duty at post No. 558 was directing traffic. Hearing gunshots in the street and then seeing a young man in a suit running frantically in pain, followed by a thug chasing him, he quickly drew his gun and fired, intending to capture the thug. Unexpectedly, there were accomplices on either side of the police officer watching. After the police officer on duty fired one shot, the thug next to him also fired three consecutive shots, all hitting the police officer in the legs. As a result, the police officer on duty also fell to the ground in front of the Mei Zuishi Shoe Store. The two thugs then took the opportunity to escape east along Hankou Road. By the time police officers on duty from Fuzhou Road, Nanjing Road, and other places arrived to chase them, they had already escaped without a trace. They immediately reported to the Old Zhabei Police Station and used an ambulance to rush Chen and the wounded police officer to the Shanghai Municipal Council Hospital for treatment. At the same time, they notified the Municipal Police Bureau and the police agencies in various districts to jointly track down the murderers. However, Chen Qing's injuries were very serious, coupled with excessive blood loss, so his life was in great danger. As for why he was suddenly attacked, it is not yet known. However, it is known that Chen was very capable in his work, and it is possible that he incurred resentment because of this, leading to this tragedy.

Sailboat Collides with Ferry, Resulting in Drowning; Police Officer Zhou Hanqing Tragically Drowns; Night Ferries Should Pay Attention to Safety

Around 9:00 PM the night before last, Zhao Fulin, a local ferryman of Dongjiadu Ferry, was carrying passengers from the Puxi dock, turning the boat back to Pudong, and sailed to the center of the river. Suddenly, a white sailboat came flying from the north, encountering the ferry. In the darkness, they were unable to avoid each other, and the front of the sailboat went straight into the front of the ferry. Three ferry passengers standing at the bow of the boat were pushed into the river due to the higher bow of the sailboat. In that instant, the offending sailboat was stopped by other ferry passengers. Meanwhile, they tried to rescue those who fell into the water. Two people, Yang Xiaohong from Shandong and an unknown person, were rescued on the spot. However, Zhou Hanqing (29 years old), a native of Tianjin, who was a police officer in the household registration office of the Third Precinct of the Third District in Pudong, drowned after falling into the water due to his large size.

The ferry owner, Zhao Fulin, and the ship's crew, Mao Lang, brought the sailboat captain, Chen Afu, and sailor, Li Chongde, along with the ship to Pudong, and reported the incident to the police on duty. Both parties, along with three witnesses, were taken to the Third Precinct of the Third District. First, the ferry side described the circumstances of the collision. Then, the sailboat captain stated that the owner of the boat was an Englishman, working as a comprador in Anli Foreign Firm. Today, the owner went to Minhang for a trip and instructed me to sail the boat back from Minhang at night. Unexpectedly, the disaster suddenly occurred in the middle of the journey.

Director Dong of the station, considering that the case occurred on the water, transferred both parties and witnesses to the Water Police General Team yesterday for interrogation. The offending sailboat was temporarily detained for investigation. As for the deceased, he was returning from shopping in Puxi at the time and was caught in a sudden misfortune, leaving behind a wife and two children, who were impoverished and extremely miserable. However, the police officer was not wearing his uniform at the time, but a blue serge long gown. The body had not yet been recovered as of last night.

Inspection Report of the China Land Reclamation Bank

The China Land Reclamation Bank's Currency Issuance Reserve Inspection Report states: The China Land Reclamation Bank's issuance treasury and business treasury have always been completely separated. According to the bank's articles of association, the cash reserve should be above 70% and the guarantee reserve should be above 30%. On the 9th of this month, accountant Wang Zikang, together with Xu Jiying and Xu Busun, representatives of the board of directors and supervisors, inspected the results as follows: the total amount of convertible notes issued was 6,811,000 silver dollars. The total amount of convertible note reserves was 6,811,000 silver dollars, including 5,727,000 silver dollars in cash reserves and 1,084,000 silver dollars in guarantee reserves. The cash reserve accounts for slightly more than 84%, and the guarantee reserve accounts for slightly less than 16%. This report is made accordingly.

Resolution of Price Dispute in the Tobacco Exchange Industry

The Shanghai Tobacco Exchange Association previously suffered excessive losses in retail stores due to soaring foreign prices, making it difficult to maintain business. On April 29, it invited representatives from various industries throughout the city, and the joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees decided to reprint the price list and distribute it to all stores for compliance. On May 20, the Fuxin Company mistakenly advertised the ten-pack of Holmes cigarettes for 160 copper cash per pack in a certain newspaper, although it was corrected in the newspaper on the 21st. However, the industry believed that the company deliberately sabotaged the market. The newspaper advertisement and the sentence on the ten-pack seal were deemed to be insulting and damaging to the industry's reputation. The association was requested to negotiate, demanding that the company apologize to the industry, issue a corrected statement in the newspaper, and replace the old seal. Ge Yunfu, the business director of the company, agreed to the request and immediately complied. The price of the Si Taifei cigarettes of Yongtaihe Company was also mistakenly published, and Hong Yisheng was elected to negotiate with them. They expressed sympathy. The letter from Fuxin Tobacco Company to the Executive Committee is recorded below: Dear Sirs, Due to the harsh wording on the seal of Holmes cigarettes, it has caused misunderstandings among our colleagues. We are grateful for your association's mediation. Our company will stop using the old seal and both parties can explain the situation. Our company, in addition to complying with the original agreement, would like to express our sincere gratitude to your association for its impartial mediation. The dispute has been resolved. The price list for June was approved for printing and distribution on the 5th, and all stores will be notified to implement it on the 15th.

Calligraphy and Painting News

Lingnan Tan Yunshan Gives Away a Thousand Books, Couplets, and Fans

Mr. Tan Yunshan, former secretary of the Guangxi Provincial Governor's Office, is famous in Guangdong and Guangxi for his Wei Bei calligraphy. In the tenth year of the Republic, he retired from politics and traveled to Shanghai, residing in the humble Shanghai area, not asking about national affairs, but using commerce as a pastime, and indulging in poetry and wine in his spare time. In the past, he served as an editorial board member of the Chinese Calligraphy and Painting Preservation Association's National Essence Monthly and as the editor of the Yangjingbang Newspaper. He occasionally painted for friends, and those who obtained his work regarded it as invaluable. From then on, his name became famous throughout the north and south of the Yangtze River, and he was hailed as Tan Wei Bei. His calligraphy is like charging horses and masts in the wind, beyond comparison in its soaring momentum, and like dew, flowers, smoke, and the moon, unforgettable in its charming form. In the twelfth year of the Republic, he met the old man Fan Fanshan, who especially admired his work and revised its ink tone, further enhancing his reputation. In recent years, he has been overworked and often feels weak, so he often avoids painting by pleading illness. Recently, because of the emergence of strange characters, which are harmful to elegance and make scholars at a loss, he has risen again and re-established his connection with the community through calligraphy, also with the intention of guiding later learners to the right track. He is giving away a thousand books, couplets, and fans. Each couplet or fan surface costs only one dollar for ink. If you want him to write the "New Life Covenant," each item costs two dollars for ink. The collection point is Chen Xiaozhe, Xianshi Insurance Company, No. 303 Nanjing Road, Zhejiang Road, Shanghai. Items can be picked up in three days in this city and five days in other cities.

Since both parties were from the same hometown, they did not pay much attention at first. Unexpectedly, in the first month of this year, Xing Chan often came to entangle with Jian Ci. Shou Leng was afraid of being implicated and ordered Jian Ci to move to another place. However, Xing Chan still came to cause trouble, so Shou Leng reported it to the Public Security Bureau for investigation. Reading Q&A

On the Contradictions of Life (3)

In the past two days, we discussed the roots of the contradictions of life and the manifestation of the contradictions of life in terms of thought and thought. Today, we will further explain the contradictions between thought and action, and between action and action: The author emphasizes the following discussion on "how to overcome behavioral contradictions." It will be published tomorrow. Readers are especially asked to pay attention to tomorrow's conclusion. Editor

4. Contradictions between thought and action, contradictions between action and action

We often see a person speaking beautifully and writing beautifully, but when asked about his behavior, a dual personality inevitably emerges. We also often see a person's actions being inconsistent from beginning to end. These are the problems that this section will explain.

This phenomenon is particularly evident in the lives of modern people. Modern people mostly express dissatisfaction with the current society, so they can often accept a more progressive side in terms of thought, and oppose the rotten side. But in action, they remain conservative and cannot move forward, clearly displaying a dual personality. They sometimes feel distressed by this split and have tried to reconcile or overcome it, but very few can truly achieve unity of thought and action. This is undoubtedly due to their special living conditions. A philanthropist can only have some superficial sympathy, but he cannot live in poverty and mingle with the hungry. His understanding of poverty is not gained from real life; he is standing in the position of a spectator, feeling a little unbearable. Therefore, in the phenomenon of contradiction between thought and action, the development of thought cannot be completely denied, but it is bound to end when it develops to a certain limit (that is, exceeding his life's tolerance). Looking back at the Xinhai Revolution, we can thoroughly understand this. During the Xinhai Revolution, there was no shortage of people who accepted revolutionary theory, but those who could participate in practice were undeniably few. Especially for those who shared hardships with Mr. Huang Kecheng on that day, and later retreated, "I agree with the revolution, but because I am not used to a wandering, dangerous life, I cannot sacrifice so much, I cannot completely abandon my private life's happiness, so I cannot help but withdraw from revolutionary action." This is indeed an honest confession. In fact, people like this cannot be said to have a deep understanding of the revolution. They are detached from practice and speak empty words about revolution. Therefore, even if he is willing to delve into theory, the result will still have a certain limit, or he will turn into metaphysics.

When it comes to reading, we can also find similar phenomena. Luo Jun is a young man who loves literature. According to his letter, he often feels his own superficiality and wants to put in some effort in social science to deepen his understanding of society. However, his thoughts are like this, but his actions are completely different. He is not used to reading rigid social sciences, and he has no interest. This is naturally not accidental. This still needs to be explained by Luo Jun's life. Luo Jun's life is very comfortable. His dissatisfaction with the status quo and his desire to understand society are vague. He is completely living a leisurely life. He has developed lazy habits. His dissatisfaction is nothing more than a superficial stimulus from the current international situation and the Chinese national crisis. His real life, that is, his personal private life, is still safe and sound. He has never experienced the struggle of life, and naturally will not feel the need to acquire a set of strategies for the struggle of life. Studying literature was originally a pastime for him. The so-called desire to understand society is nothing more than a superficial impression, a temporary excitement. Some people may say that this is due to habit, but that is not the case. Even habit must be explained by the social living environment.

The unification of thought and action can also be explained by other social reasons. For example, take the common masturbation of unmarried young people. Everyone who masturbates knows the harm of masturbation. In terms of thought, they are probably all anti-masturbationists! In terms of action, they are just doing the opposite. This is a commonly recognized fact, and it has been typically depicted in Mr. Yu Dafu's "Sinking." This contradictory phenomenon is certainly related to physiological aspects. In fact, the creation of this morbid state still goes back to the social system (especially habits such as asceticism). Because this contradiction is clearly generated through social causes.

In addition, in a situation of excessive oppression or terror, the split between thought and action is often promoted. For example, in Western history, the Holy Alliance's great reaction and the Tsarist Russia's great reaction in 1905 caused many people to hide in various areas of life, causing their thoughts to grow in a winding way.

In short, the contradiction between thought and action is roughly caused by the insufficient leap forward of social practice and people's understanding, which causes the split between people's thoughts and actions. Thought often goes ahead, and action cannot catch up, as well as the result of many other objective reasons.

As for the contradiction between action and action, this can be explained by the leap forward and backward of thought. This is the most superficial aspect of the contradiction of life. We only need to look at the changes in social practice, and those that change with it. We can often see that some people are used to taking off one piece of clothing and putting on another piece of completely different colors. This is not surprising. People's lives are originally changing all the time. Even so, a person's change also has a certain limit. The thing that determines this limit is still the special social living environment in which the individual lives.

The above explanation is only for the explanation of contradictions, not for the defense of contradictory phenomena. We feel that a person's life is not afraid of contradictions, and it cannot be denied that there are contradictions. What we should pay attention to is being able to make a rational explanation of the phenomenon of contradictions. We should not only explain contradictions, but also change the unreasonable contradictory phenomena in life. We should use the contradiction of the life process and use it actively to overcome the contradictions that hinder our lives. Below, we will further forcefully propose how to overcome the contradictions in behavior that are harmful to the development of our lives.

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

Reading and Playing

— Hanyun

Reading is necessary, but playing is also necessary.

Reading can increase our knowledge, and playing can gradually restore the brainpower that has been used up after playing, so these are all tasks that children need to do, but we cannot read all day long, nor can we play all day long.

Reading all day long can make our brainpower confused. Because of the confusion of brainpower, we cannot get any benefit from the books we want to read; playing all day long, even if it wastes our time, we cannot get any knowledge. Only by reading for a while and then playing for a while can we fully gain knowledge, but our brainpower will not be confused at all.

Children! Do you read or play all day long? Or do you read for a while and then play? This is a very noteworthy question, and you should pay attention to it!

But at the same time, children should also pay attention to whether the games they play or the books they read are useful?

Selfishness

— Long Shi

Little friends! Don't you love listening to stories? Let me tell you one!

A fox was caught by hunters. In order to escape the iron cage, its tail was cut off by the cage door. After returning to the mountain, it saw that all its peers had thick tails, and felt extremely ashamed of its own defect. If it could, it would rather have died in the iron cage. Finally, it came up with the best remedy: to convene a meeting with the purpose of asking the other foxes to cut off their tails like it did.

"This is unconscious," it said at the meeting. "My actions are now very convenient and comfortable. If I hadn't tried it, I would never have believed my words were right. Everyone says that a tail is an ugly and useless thing. Why do we all have such long tails? Brothers! Cut off your tails like me, and you will get many benefits!"

An old fox stepped forward and said, "Friend! I've thought about it again and again. You don't have to ask us to give up our tails. It would be better if you had the chance to grow yours back."

Little friends! The story above clearly tells us that selfishness can harm the public interest, and selfish people are enemies of the public.

Summer Hygiene

— Bo Zhen

The giant wheel of the seasons is gradually turning from the mild spring to the hot summer.

The enemies of people in summer – flies, mosquitoes, and all other microorganisms – some have already appeared, and some are still breeding.

People, the spirits of all things, are thinking about how to resist and eliminate enemies. This is called hygiene. This is something that all children should know.

(1) Personal hygiene:

Active aspects: Do not drink cold water. Do not eat food that flies have already eaten. Food must be placed under a cover. Do not eat overnight, spoiled food. Mosquito coils and fly swatters are also indispensable items in summer.

Passive aspects: Do not have dirty water accumulating in jars. Feces jars should have lids. If there are mosquito larvae in the water, eliminate them quickly. Install screens on all doors and windows in the house.

(2) Public hygiene:

Active aspects: Service-oriented social groups, such as youth associations, should pay a high price to buy dead flies. Buy fly swatters and distribute them to the poor who have no money. At the same time, establish epidemic hospitals so that poor people who contract epidemic diseases and have no money for treatment can receive free medical care in the hospital.

Passive aspects: In winter, people should be sent to collect the eggs of flies and mosquitoes and completely eliminate the eggs. Do not allow spoiled items, such as watermelon rinds and dead dogs and cats, to accumulate and be discarded in rivers and streets.

The above are all important measures for summer hygiene.

Early Rising by Wu Yongkang, Student of Taicang Jiao Yan Corner Elementary School

Get up early! You must get up early; get up to see the sun, the sun is a good color, see the moon is about to disappear, a curved line like an eyebrow, see strips of colorful clouds.

The patterns on each strip are exquisite, the flowers emit fragrance, the birds chirp,

I get up in the morning, wash my face, and carry my schoolbag to school. The teacher says, "It's really good that you can get up early!"

"Mother Frog"

— Su Su

Originally, Mother Frog was afraid of the cold and hid in a mud cave, not daring to come out. Later, Miss Spring knocked on her door, and she peeked her head out to look. "Ah! How beautiful! Miss," Mother Frog was very happy, and at the same time called out to the big frogs and little frogs!

Miss Spring was very happy and took the big frogs, little frogs, and Mother Frog on a trip to the lush green wheat field. As soon as they arrived in the wheat field, they saw Wheat Brother being bullied by many, many little bugs. Mother Frog was so angry that her eyes were like lanterns. She jumped over and swallowed the unfair little bugs one by one. She also said to Wheat Brother, "I will always be your guard from now on, protecting your health." From then on, Wheat Brother was very happy, nodding from time to time in the fields.

One day, Mother Frog came out of the mud field to bathe in the pond and saw many small bugs in black clothes with tails. Mother Frog thought, "These must be enemies that harm rice and wheat. She planned how to kill them." Unexpectedly, at this moment, the little bugs all ran over, shouting "Mommy! Mommy!" Mother Frog saw that they were all wearing black clothes and sternly said, "I don't recognize you if you don't wear green clothes like me!" The little bugs were very sad and sat in the pond, worried. Just then, Miss Spring passed by, and the little bugs asked Miss Spring, "Where can we find green clothes?" Miss Spring said in surprise, "Your feet haven't grown out yet, so how can your clothes turn green?" The little bugs heard that their feet hadn't grown out, so they exercised their lower limbs every day.

More than twenty days passed, and the little bugs' feet finally grew out, and their black clothes also turned green. The little bugs were very happy and went to the mud field to find their mother.

A Deflated Rubber Ball After Being Heated by the Fire

— Kong Jie

Bao Ge and Mao Di found a deflated rubber ball. Because it couldn't bounce, they couldn't play with it.

Just then, their older brother walked by. After hearing what they said, he put the ball on the fire to heat it. Before long, it had turned into a hard and bouncy ball.

After a while, Bao Ge and Mao Di ran back and said to their brother, "Look, this ball is even more deflated than before." As they said this, they handed the ball to their brother.

Their brother took the ball, smiled, and said, "I was just teasing you. Don't be upset. I'll buy you a new one tomorrow. Do you know why this ball became hard and then deflated after being heated?"

The two shook their heads together.

Their brother then continued, "Now, we know that everything in the world is made up of many tiny particles called molecules. These molecules are so small that even a high-powered microscope can't see them. When we put the ball on the fire to heat it, we are making the air molecules inside the ball move faster. When molecules move very fast, they inevitably collide and push each other. The result of the molecules pushing outward in all directions is that the ball becomes larger. However, at this time, some of the air is squeezed out and escapes through the small gaps in the ball. When the ball cools down, the molecules also move slowly, so the ball deflates. Also, because some of the air has been squeezed out of the ball, the ball is now even more deflated."

The two brothers understood the reason and nodded together. They happily followed their brother to buy a new ball.

Fathers' and Brothers' Mistakes

— Yangtze River

Years ago, I read an essay by Lu Xun, which said that Mr. Lu Xun had torn up a kite belonging to his younger brother, Mr. Zhou Zuoren, when he was a child. At that time, Mr. Lu Xun believed that flying kites was a useless activity for hooligan children, and as an older brother, he should be responsible for correcting it. However, after he read some books on child psychology, he realized that his previous interference with his younger brother was very unreasonable. In his middle age, he said to his younger brother, seemingly with a hint of guilt, but Mr. Zhou Zuoren had completely forgotten about it. The general idea of the article is like this, and the author further expressed at the end that all fathers and brothers in the world should correct mistakes like his. His intention is admirable. Before reading that article, I had indeed made the same mistake as Mr. Lu Xun. I had torn up many kites belonging to my second and third younger brothers so severely. But later I realized it, and I even criticized my second younger brother for following in my footsteps and tearing up the kites of my fifth and sixth younger brothers. Recently, there was a kite competition in Nanjing, and Chairman Lin and others had prizes. This shows the grand occasion of the competition. Why did Chairman Lin and others promote kites? There must be very sufficient reasons. From this, I would like to specifically point out that flying kites is very beneficial to the physical and mental development of children. Innumerable fathers and brothers in the mainland, please immediately correct that mistake of unwarranted interference!

The Progress of the Steamship Industry in the Past Two Hundred Years 丨From the Most Primitive Steamships to Modern Steamships丨

— He Gongchao

1. The earliest steamboat 丨 Hull's tugboat (1737) 2. Jouffroy d'Abbans' steamboat (1783) 3. Fitch's paddle steamboat (1786) 4. Symington's double-hulled steamboat (1788) 5. Symington's Charlotte Dundas steamboat (1801) 6. The first successful steamboat: Fulton's Clermont (1807) 7. Bell's Comet steamboat (1812) 8. The Savannah, which crossed the Atlantic (1819) 9. The Sirius steamboat (1838) 10. The Great Western steamboat (same as above) 11. The Britannia (1840) 12. The Great Britain steamboat (1844) 13. The modern Mauritania (after 1907)

The first steamboat was made by a man named Hull, but its machinery took up most of the space in the cabin, so it could not carry cargo or passengers and could only be used as a tugboat. In the nearly fifty years after Hull, the steamship manufacturing industry did not make much progress, but after a while, people in various countries became more interested in studying steamships. We saw the various experiments of the British and French, and we also saw Fulton's Clermont. Fulton was American. He made the first successful steamboat. The Savannah crossed the Atlantic in 1819, but it only used steam power for the first and last parts of the journey. The middle part of the journey was still sailed by sails. The ships that crossed the Atlantic purely by steam power were two British ships: the Sirius and the Great Western. They sailed from England to New York within a few hours of each other. From that time on, the progress of steamships was very fast, and their size was always increasing. Modern steamships are no longer comparable to the primitive and small steamships of the past.

Water Bird

— Shi Yusheng

Little friends, have you ever seen that kind of bird flying along the golden waves on the coast of the big river? They look so leisurely and comfortable. Little friends, you are wrong! They have extremely vicious eyes and extremely cruel claws. They fly lightly, but their eyes are focused on the heart of the waves: as soon as a playful fish pokes its head out, it is caught by a claw! They cruise on the waves non-stop, and the poor fish are constantly being slaughtered by them. Little friends, what kind of bird is this? This is the water bird that the enemy is using to carry out "water bird diplomacy" against us!

Little friends, the enemy is insidiously acting as "water birds." Are we willing to be fish?

The Fiercest Animal in the Sea

— Bing Yu

Speaking of the largest animal on earth, of course, the whale is the first to be mentioned. The length of a whale can reach thirty meters. However, once such a huge whale is attacked by an orca, it is useless. The orca is a type of dolphin whose sharp teeth in both the upper and lower jaws often bite the whale's body into pulverized bones and death. Orcas in the sea like to unite with their own kind, forming groups to specialize in harming whales. Therefore, when whales see orcas, they often desperately flee, mistakenly swimming to the seashore and being caught by fishermen.

The stingray's tail is like a serrated thorn, and the tip of the tail emits extremely poisonous venom. Coming into contact with this venom is fatal. When fishermen catch stingrays, they must first cut off their tails to prevent being harmed. Stingrays have venom to defend against enemies and serrated thorns, but they are no match for sharks or sharks. Because the sharp teeth of sharks and sharks can chew the serrated tail into pieces. This means that there are always stronger enemies, and no one can be arrogant or complacent.

Shipworms are even more dangerous than orcas, stingrays, sharks, and sharks. They are very small in size but can destroy large ships. They are called shipworms. The body of the worm is covered with a limestone shell. This kind of pest, regardless of whether the ship's body is made of wood or iron, if it is attached to it, it can gradually drill the ship's body into a honeycomb-like hole. Therefore, shipbuilders around the world have researched methods to prevent and eliminate them. In addition to wrapping the ship's body with iron, they also apply insect-repellent medicine. Barnacles are cone-shaped shellfish. These barnacles often attach to the surroundings of warships at sea, reducing the ship's speed. This is because the bottom of the ship is covered with layers of barnacle shells weighing dozens of tons. The ship's movement is therefore restricted. Although shipbuilders apply poisonous oil to the ship's body, the digestive organs of young barnacles are not yet developed, and no matter what kind of poisonous oil is used, they will not be infected.

Village Little Friends' Correspondence to Send Off Spring

— Zi Ming

Dear little friends:

Spring came hastily, but now it is secretly leaving. Its arrival decorated our earth very brightly and beautifully. We are grateful for it and welcome it. Now that it is leaving, are we just going to let it go silently? Isn't that too lonely? So, since there was a welcome at the beginning, there should be a farewell at the end, so as not to let down its painstaking efforts in building nature.

How do we express it? Poets and writers use wine and pens to bid farewell. We are ambitious and progressive people who don't passively do boring things. In the previous letter, it was said that "youth symbolizes children." We can't help but feel sorry about this! Watching spring come, grow old, and leave. Our farewell to spring only has a warm childlike heart, containing the deep meaning of "farewell." At this time, the only thing to do is to follow the passage of time and find our future broad road.

Spring has left, and the beautiful apricot blossoms and the fresh peach blossoms have long been taken away by it. The cuckoos are crying for it, and their sad voices penetrate the hearts of travelers. The god of thunder is also firing cannons, indicating farewell? Or anger? Friends! Can you tell?

Friends! The "spring" that cannot be retained has left! Remember!

Small Fountain

— Bai Yi

This is a very fun and simple science game:

Method: First, fill a medium-sized glass bottle with about three-quarters of clear water, and then plug it with a cork with a hollow glass tube inserted in it, making sure that one end of the tube is close to the bottom of the bottle; seal it tightly, preferably with sealing wax. Then, take a larger glass bottle and bake it over a candle flame for three to four minutes, and then cover it over the small glass bottle. Soon, we can see the water gradually rising and spraying out from inside the tube.

Reason: After the large glass bottle is baked on the fire, the air inside expands due to the heat, and then a part of it escapes out of the bottle. After the large bottle is covered over the small bottle, because the pressure is smaller, the air in the small bottle rushes out, and the pressure above the small bottle decreases, so it also sprays out, because water originally has a force that pushes upwards.

When we play this game, it is best to spread a few pieces of absorbent paper under the small bottle, because this will prevent the sprayed water from flowing in all directions, and it will also prevent outside air from entering the large bottle.

Statement: The author's name was omitted from the first article "How to Read Books" in the previous issue. After investigation, it was written by Mr. Gu Xuefan. We hereby declare it.

An Extra Handle on the Shady Tree

— Xiao Jianqing

1. A cat went to the table to look for food. 2. He saw a vase and crawled into it. 3. Xiao Ming came over and was happy to see that the vase had an extra handle. 4. He lifted the vase by the handle and was startled. 5. The vase broke, the cat ran away, and Xiao Ming cried loudly. 6. His older sister patted Xiao Ming and said, "Why are you so rash?"

Ministry of Education Formulates Holiday Measures for Social Education Institutions

The Ministry of Education, according to the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education, submitted a request from the Provincial Nanjing Public Education Hall for instructions on the holiday measures for social education institutions for approval and compliance. On the 9th, the Ministry of Education instructed the said department as follows: "We have received the submission. The holidays of social education institutions should be handled in accordance with the following provisions: (1) During severe cold and hot weather, they may take turns to rest, but may not take holidays. The dates shall be separately stipulated by the educational administrative organs of each province and city and the national social education organs according to local conditions, and shall be reported to the Ministry of Education for record. (2) Sundays and commemorative days shall not be holidays and shall be made up on the following day. (3) The New Year shall not be a holiday and shall be made up from January 4th to 6th. You should immediately inform and instruct them to comply with this order."

Memorial Wu Scholarship to Cultivate Diplomatic Talents

Regarding the memorial for Mr. Wu Tiyun, the Memorial Wu Tiyun Committee has now been established. The committee is a permanent organization dedicated to discussing and handling matters related to the Wu memorial. According to the committee's news yesterday, more than 15,000 yuan has been raised for the Wu Scholarship Fund. The predetermined amount is 20,000 yuan, not much difference, and it will be fully raised soon. Of the 15,000 yuan raised so far, 10,000 yuan has been allocated and deposited in the Shanghai Bank with an annual interest rate of 1%, and the interest will be used as scholarships. It can be implemented in the autumn of this year. How to allocate it will be decided after a meeting. More than 5,000 yuan will be deposited into the bank to earn interest after the full amount is raised. The Memorial Wu Tiyun Committee authorities believe that Wu was a diplomat during his lifetime, and intend to use this scholarship to cultivate diplomatic talents, but it has not yet been fully decided. As for the establishment of Wu's bronze [statue], it is already in preparation. The location will definitely be in Shanghai, and eight or nine out of ten will be erected in the city center. All the methods are in preparation.

Minsheng Girls' School to Establish Summer School

Minsheng Girls' School, located at the intersection of Avenue Joffre and Rue Amiral Bayle in the French Concession, has established a summer school specifically for primary and secondary school students in order to solve the problems of further education and advanced studies. The school specializes in enrolling students with primary and junior high school levels so that they can be admitted to senior high school after tutoring. Therefore, the curriculum strives to be practical. The school also compiles and statistics the past national junior and senior high school entrance examination questions so that it can simplify teaching and enable students to gain a considerable concept of major subjects in a short period of time. The curriculum is divided into Chinese (writing, reading, further education guidance, and general knowledge of Chinese studies), mathematics (geometry, algebra, and arithmetic), and English (reader, grammar, and conversation). The tutoring time is from 7 am to 10 am every morning, for a total of six weeks. It is also reported that the school is scheduled to start on July 5.

Sports News

Jiangda Volleyball Team Wins Championship, Straight Three Victories Over Jinan, Central University Jinling Semifinals All North

(Nanjing, 9th - Jiangda Volleyball Championship Semifinals, 9th morning, Fudan defeated Jinda three to zero, Jinan defeated Central University one to zero. Finals between the two schools were held at Central University at 3 p.m. Qiu Guangxiao of Fudan and Xu Heng of Jinan were both famous players who attended the Far Eastern Games, each showing their skills, which was extremely exciting. Fudan won the championship with an average talent, winning three games in a row with twenty-one to thirteen, twenty-one to thirteen, and twenty-one to sixteen.

The Jiangda Volleyball Championship held two semi-finals in Beijing yesterday morning. One was Fudan vs. Jinling at the Jinda playground, and the result was three to zero, Fudan won. The other was Jinan vs. Central University at the Central University playground, and the result was three to zero, Jinan won. The situation of the semi-finals is recorded separately below.

Jinan wins against Central University. Central University is a well-established team in Beijing. Today, when they met the Jinan team, which has Xu Heng and other athletes who attended the Far Eastern Games, they felt inferior. After referee Lu Song'en announced the start of the battle, Jinan took the lead from beginning to end. In the first game, Jinan took the lead with eleven to five. After changing sides, although Central University tried hard to struggle, Jinan won the first game with twenty-one to eleven. In the second game, Jinan also took the lead with eleven to seven and won the second game with twenty-one to fifteen. In the final game, Jinan still took the lead with eleven to two and won the right to the final. This time, the Central University team's blocks were too loose, and the kills were not far enough, so Jinan's athlete Xu Heng took the opportunity to kill the ball. The three games ended in just fifty minutes.

Fudan wins against Jinling. Fudan is the volleyball leader of Shanghai universities, and Jinling is the champion of previous sessions in Beijing. When the two heroes met, the audience expected a bloody battle. The game started at 9 am yesterday morning at the Jinda Stadium, and the referee was Zhang Xinfu.
