Notice to Swimming Trainees

Swimming is the best and only sport suitable for the current summer season. Because swimming exercises the entire body, it not only promotes balanced development, but also deepens breathing, strengthens nerves, and develops organs, meeting various health requirements. However, water is extremely dangerous, and without adequate swimming skills, there is a risk of drowning, not to mention competing and winning. Therefore, to succeed in swimming and consistently win medals, in addition to diligent practice, reading renowned swimming books is essential. The Qinfen Bookstore at 392 Rue du Père Robert, French Concession, caters to the needs of the times by engaging well-known domestic swimming experts to compile and write various swimming books. Details are listed below: (1) *The Art of Swimming Success* by British swimming expert Hedges, translated by Wu Futong, and proofread by swimming expert Yu Binqi. The book is divided into nine major chapters, each with many sections. Chapter 1: Befriending Water; Chapter 2: Crawl Stroke Technique; Chapter 3: Overarm Stroke Technique; Chapter 4: Backstroke Technique; Chapter 5: Diving Technique; Chapter 6: Water Games; Chapter 7: Lifesaving Techniques; Chapter 8: Swimming Competitions; Chapter 9: All-Around Swimming and Artistic Swimming. Includes dozens of valuable posture photographs. Printed on high-quality paper in a 32mo format, thick volume, priced at 60 cents, special offer at 10% discount. This is a must-have book for swimming enthusiasts, providing detailed guidance, especially for beginners. Purchasing this book for reference is highly recommended. (2) *Swimming Training Methods* by renowned domestic swimming expert Qian Yiqin, a compilation of carefully gathered experiences, with an inscription "The Art of Observing the Sea" by Shen Siliang, Secretary-General of the National Sports Advancement Association. The book is divided into three parts: Upper, Middle, and Lower. The Upper part, Swimming, has ten chapters, each divided into sections. Chapter 1: Introduction to Swimming; Chapter 2: Basic Swimming Exercises; Chapter 3: Sidestroke; Chapter 4: Single-Arm Overwater Sidestroke; Chapter 5: Double-Arm Alternating Overwater Stroke; Chapter 6: Crawl Stroke; Chapter 7: Backstroke; Chapter 8: Breaststroke; Chapter 9: Distance Floating and Treading Water; Chapter 10: Competitive Swimming. The Middle part, Diving, has Chapter 11: Basic Diving Techniques; Chapter 12: Artistic Diving. The Lower part, Lifesaving, has Chapter 13: Lifesaving General Theory; Chapter 14: Practice of Escape and Carrying Methods; Chapter 15: Artificial Respiration. Chapter 16: Swimming and Lifesaving Tests. Includes dozens of copperplate prints of performance postures for readers to practice following the illustrations. Printed on woodfree paper, hardbound, a thick volume, priced at 2.40 yuan, special offer at 10% discount. This book emphasizes teaching methods, with each method using commands, for swimming instructors. Yu Binqi proofread, Chapter 1: The Meaning of Swimming; Chapter 2: Equipment for Elementary School Swimming; Chapter 3: Swimming Technical Training; Chapter 4: Instructor Guidelines. Each chapter also includes multiple posture diagrams. Printed on high-quality Swedish paper, 32mo format, priced at 30 cents, special offer at 10% discount. This book focuses on swimming methods for elementary school students, edited according to the new curriculum standards promulgated by the Ministry of Education, and is essential reading for elementary school teachers. (4) Recently, graduates from the physical education department of Zhongda University have translated *Women's Swimming Training Methods*, which guides women's swimming, and has been proofread by Hao Gengsheng and Wu Yunrui, and is currently being printed. Also, *Swimming Rules* priced at 8 cents per copy. All the above books are excellent reading materials for the summer season. The bookstore at 277 Sima Road also sells these books at the same price.

Women's Garden, Issue 17

A Female Teacher's Hopes

— Shi Yan

Today's children are the future masters of the nation and the most important people in the Chinese nation's rejuvenation movement. These national masters, who bear a significant mission, are now receiving moral, intellectual, and physical education in schools, preparing their strong bodies, noble personalities, and productive skills. The nation's prosperity or decline in the future depends on the effectiveness of the current school education. The prerequisites for increasing the effectiveness of school education are a beautiful school environment, sufficient funding, appropriate teaching materials, and good teachers. The first three are inanimate, and only teachers are animate. Therefore, the transformation of the environment, the allocation of funds, and the selection of teaching materials all rely on animate teachers. From this perspective, the responsibility of teachers is extremely significant!

As for the current life of teachers? Let's take a look at Shanghai, the most developed place in education. The rest can be imagined. According to the Education Bureau's survey results, two-thirds of Shanghai's elementary school teachers' living expenses are above 60 yuan, which is far from the Ministry's standard salary. As a result, those who change their minds are everywhere. The daily working hours often exceed twelve hours (including both in and out of the classroom), which impairs their health and affects their work efficiency. In particular, female teachers are burdened by household chores such as raising children and caring for the elderly, menstrual difficulties, physiological abnormalities during pregnancy, and lack of rest before and after childbirth, resulting in even higher rates of illness and death. Due to low salaries and heavy workloads, further education is simply out of the question.

In summary, the responsibility of teachers is so great. Therefore, my hopes for teachers are: (1) Cultivation of a noble personality, (2) Training of a strong physique, (3) In-depth study of profound knowledge. The life of teachers is so difficult. Therefore, my hopes for the authorities are: (1) Increase salaries and avoid arrears, (2) Reduce workload, (3) Stipulate working and rest hours, (4) Limit the number of students, (5) Provide pensions, (6) The Health Bureau should provide diagnosis and treatment for teachers without charging medical fees, (7) Free transportation, (8) Discounts on book purchases (9) Free admission and exemption from examinations for lectures at universities or research institutes and other academic institutions, (10) Dispatch them to domestic and foreign educational inspections, (11) Teacher nurseries, (12) Rest before and after childbirth, (13) Menstrual leave, (14) The establishment of more teacher positions (15) Independent funding for education.

In this way, teachers can have a professional spirit, have the opportunity to strive for further education, and devote their full energy to experiments. This is not only for the benefit of the teachers themselves, but also for the benefit of children and the nation. Written on Teachers' Day, year 23.

The Mother of Children

— Xian

She woke up, waking from a dream. The moonlight shone on her desolately, shining on the round and clear eyes of Ning Ge'er in the photo hanging on the wall. The children stared at her foolishly, as if they wanted to cry.

Xiang was sleeping next to her, having kicked off the quilt; muttering in his sleep. She sat up, gently taking the quilt and covering Xiang; then lay down again, sighing, "Ah, where is the beautiful dream?"

Remembering the past: When Xiang entered kindergarten, Ning Ge'er always cried and made a fuss wanting to go with her sister. At that time, Xiang was already four years old; Ning Ge'er was only two years old; Yuan Yuan was just born two months ago. Every day, she had to feed Yuan Yuan milk: make beautiful clothes for the children, make delicious dishes; bathe the children... Busy, with no time to think about her own comfort and health. Her body gradually weakened, often with headaches and backaches. But for the sake of the children, she was not sad. She had a hope, hoping for a beautiful and happy family.

The children were so lovely: That one time, Xiang's school held a "Mother's Meeting," and she brought Ning Ge'er to the meeting. Xiang performed "White Rabbit" and "Little Sparrow in the Tree." Wearing a rabbit's hat, carrying a rabbit's skin; wearing a sparrow's hat and shining with a sparrow's tail. She hadn't expected that four-year-old Xiang would listen to the rhythm of the piano, follow the order of the performance, and step to the beat of the music: performing lively and innocently on stage! Later, when giving out prizes, Xiang's teacher gave Xiang a small leather ball, and Xiang was a little embarrassed to accept it and hesitated; Ning Ge'er stood up from his visitor seat, walked over, and accepted it. Everyone laughed happily: How much more joyful was she?

Xiang could sing several songs; Ning Ge'er could also sing popular party songs and drizzle; Yuan Yuan could also smile. As for her, she was still making beautiful dreams all day long; dreaming of a perfect family, with children, with love. This dream seemed to be telling her in the children's songs and laughter: It will definitely come true.

Can dreams come true?

One evening at dusk, when the sun set behind the bamboo forest, she was sent to the riverbank by a man in the world. The mountains stood far away; the water flowed endlessly; her dream, like a bird that had flown away, had disappeared without a trace!

From then on, she returned to her parents' home, who could not understand her, holding her three children. Her father did not love a "modern youth," and therefore did not love a daughter who could not be a "virtuous wife and loving mother." Her stepmother only knew how to mock her with "new school" and "old school" terms, and had no sympathy for her at all! For the sake of the children and her own future life, she wanted to find "work"; but she didn't know where to start? She wanted to rely on old classmates to find a position as an elementary school teacher; but the classmates were afraid that she would not be able to educate because of the many children. Therefore, no one was willing to take the responsibility of introducing her. Later, her teacher invited her to go to the rural women's normal school to be the director of discipline. In order not to make the young children - the children who had never left her care - leave her, she had no choice but to live with her children in the school. But the ignorant students therefore attacked her and laughed at her; the colleagues also felt that having children in the school was a matter of impropriety; so the principal wanted her to rent a house outside. And the discipline personnel in the school must reside in the school for a long time; she was forced to leave the children she could not bear to leave for a moment!

She had no experience in doing things. She knew too little about "human affairs." She didn't know how to "show off" or "play tricks"; how to contact colleagues to promote herself and be supported by students. She only knew how to cultivate a kind and simple human nature with a frank and enthusiastic heart. She treated people and things with her sincere and simple nature. Therefore, she was attacked, harmed, and insulted by people everywhere. Society even suspected that she had been deceived by a man and had been an extremely disreputable, low-class concubine.

She took her children everywhere to make a living; whenever she lost her job, she took her children back to her parents' home. Her stepmother blamed her for being too bad-tempered and not being able to stay in places for long. She had no choice but to endure it. Unfortunately, her hometown encountered several bandits that year; coupled with the collapse of the countryside and the recession of commerce, the life of her parents' family also generally declined. Even her father sometimes thought about the future life of her and her children, and could not help but sigh in secret!

At this time, Xiang developed a severe case of typhoid fever. The fever was so high that she was already delirious. The bones of her whole body ached as if they were about to break apart, making her afraid to even hold her. What could she do? Living in the countryside, without money, and getting such a disease, she could only watch her die! Knowing that she had no ability to save her child, she let her family take care of the sick child in a daze. Fortunately, by chance, when the child's illness was already incurable, her aunt, who had only read some medical books and had no medical experience, saved her with medicine worth fifteen copper coins!

She had suffered too much and too greatly; she began to resent this cruel world. She hated why the world had given birth to her! She cursed why the world didn't destroy her! But the chains of life tightly bound her, leaving her no time to resent or curse. She couldn't think about the past again; she didn't dare to think about the future. For the sake of her children's future safety and happiness, she knew that she had to temporarily bear to leave her children: otherwise, she knew that the children would all perish together. So, on a morning of rainy and snowy weather, she escaped from her parents' home; abandoned her children; and with her only luggage - a grieving and courageous heart - ran far to Beiping, in the opposite direction of her hometown. She wanted to do everything in her power to save her children! But she was still making beautiful, rose-colored dreams - a beautiful family, with children, with flowers, with love...

She roamed in Beiping for a full three years. Did she still have the courage to think about these three years of wandering life? The beautiful rose-colored dreams, like birds, flew away and could never be found!

The cannon sound of September 18th awakened her from her delusion! She knew that under the claws of imperialism, everything was in a dark hell; how could her beautiful, rose-colored dreams come true? The oppressed as a whole cannot obtain a peaceful life. She would be no exception. Will the beautiful dreams still come true?

Creation

Hesitation

— Zi Gang

In the morning, Sister-in-law Sun hurried to take Second Aunt's arm and run onto the awning boat going to the city. A half-inch-long root stick shows through the center of the thick hair bun, the peach-colored face and the two women's hearts are as active as can be.

Although, in the activity is mixed with the anxiety of a wildfire burning.

Second Aunt is an experienced city goer, but this time she still couldn't put on a smiling face, looking so uncomfortable, staring warily at the calm river surface. In her heart, however, "Finding a job to do!" She said, over and over.

Sitting next to her like a wooden chicken, Sister-in-law Sun was even more uneasy. It was her first time going to the city. If she found a place to settle down, she would have to live in the city for a long time.

"Maybe this year will be a bumper year, maybe even better than last year's harvest. The fields are left unplanted..." Sister-in-law Sun looked at the green fields and trees along the shore, feeling the harmony of wind and rain, and couldn't help but think of the farming she was about to abandon and began to feel pity for it. People are used to a certain kind of life and often have a little attachment to it, especially when the other thing is already a vague uncertainty.

Second Aunt opened her experienced eyes:

"It's a waste that you can't let go, are you really going to starve to death before you give up? Last year wasn't a bumper year, we? Even if we sold our second-rate fields, it wasn't enough to pay the rent. In the end, we had to eat half and borrow half. I've figured it out."

Sister-in-law Sun frowned, thinking that Second Aunt was indeed more knowledgeable, and what she said made sense; but then she thought that Second Aunt's man was already working odd jobs in the city, coming back when the fields were busy, otherwise he would live in the city. This time, abandoning the fields to go to the city was not a big deal, but she was entrusting her fatherless children to her in-laws and going alone to climb a difficult path. Thinking about it, tears were about to fall from her eyes, so she quickly stopped them.

The people in the boat were all like her, each with a serious face, each calculating their own affairs in the city. If they knew each other, they would chat about firewood, rice, oil, and salt, mixed with seven points of sigh. Towards this hometown, they were as hesitant as towards a dilapidated temple, not knowing how to repair it, or simply destroy it.

Steamships passed the awning boats, one after another. Inside them sat the "upper-class figures" or "semi-upper-class figures" of the townships.

××

Sister-in-law Sun and Second Aunt wandered through the streets and alleys. Second Aunt searched all the brokerage shops that she knew a little bit, but couldn't find a place to stay. Every shop was full of two rows of people waiting to be hired, men and women. Some were in transit, and some were freshly arrived from the countryside. Everyone abandoned the villages and towns that could no longer produce oil and ran to find a livelihood in the city. As a result, unusually, at the beginning of the rice planting season, the brokerage shops were full of people waiting to be hired. Country folks fled to the city like bees rushing to an orchard, but the city was as dry as a skeleton.

"Keep your eyes open, put in the effort, we can do it, we're used to hardship..."

The owner of the brokerage shop wiped his sweat:

"People who just came from the countryside are even less popular, there are so many people that there's not even enough room to stay. Hurry back on the late boat!"

"Can't we just stay for one night? We only came out because we really couldn't plant the fields anymore." With impossible hopes, the two women carried their cloth bags and searched for the signs of brokerage shops on the street, their hearts both bitter and sour.

At the dock, travelers running to various places gathered, and boats of various styles were lined up in the heart of the river. Stepping on the gangplank, Sister-in-law Sun and Second Aunt trembled their legs and stepped past, squeezed in among so many people with the same fate.

Children and Sunbathing

— Geng Longgen

Of course, mothers want their children to be strong. In the minds of most Chinese mothers, they believe that the way to make their children strong is to drink more milk and eat more. Drinking milk and eating is indeed beneficial to children's health, but eating and drinking too much is harmful to their health.

Now I am going to introduce the best way to strengthen children's bodies: sunbathing.

Sunlight has been known since ancient times as something beneficial to people. However, Chinese mothers probably do not want their children to be exposed to the sun, which will cause their skin to turn black and lose the beauty of white skin.

Modern scientific research has shown that sunlight emits light and heat. These light and heat are extremely necessary for human life, and at the same time, they can treat and prevent tuberculosis and rickets in children. Therefore, it can make children's bodies strong and healthy.

Sunlight is so beneficial to people, and it does not need money to buy. It can be obtained anywhere. At the same time, sunbathing does not require any equipment. Therefore, using sunlight to strengthen children's bodies is more economical than other methods, and its effectiveness is greater than other methods. Sunlight reflects seven colors from raindrops: red, orange, yellow, green, blue, indigo, and violet. Sunlight also reflects the same seven colors as the rainbow when it passes through a prism. The red color on one side is the heat ray in sunlight. The purple color on the other side is the light ray, but on both sides, there are still rays that we cannot see. The one on the red side is called infrared, which generates a lot of heat. The one on the purple side is called ultraviolet rays; this ray not only emits light, but also contains a large amount of special qualities that can strengthen the body and help growth.

When sunlight passes through solids, the light is filtered out. When sunlight passes through transparent objects such as glass, both heat rays and light rays can pass through, but ultraviolet rays cannot. Therefore, when sunbathing, the sunlight must be able to directly shine on the skin in order to obtain the benefits of ultraviolet rays.

Ultraviolet rays can give people strong bones and healthy muscles, and can also help growth and nutrition. When this ray is mixed with the heat rays in sunlight, it forms a dark brown pigment on the skin. Sunlight passes through this pigment, and ultraviolet rays can fully enter the body.

This ray also has the effect of killing bacteria, resisting infectious diseases, treating and preventing tuberculosis and rickets in children.

The best place for sunbathing is outdoors in hot weather, and indoors in cold weather. In cold weather, you should face the open window, and other doors and windows should be closed to prevent drafts. However, in extremely cold weather, difficulties may arise. It is said that there is now a special glass that allows ultraviolet rays to penetrate.

The duration of sunbathing should also be determined by the cold or hot weather. In cold weather, it should be done at noon, and in hot weather, it should be done in the morning and evening. Otherwise, it will be too cold or too hot, which may cause illness. The duration should also be regulated. It is best for children to make sunbathing a habit, just like brushing their teeth and washing their bodies. Also, it is best to have children play games and exercise at the same time when sunbathing.

Sunlight is more valuable than any tonic. I hope mothers with children will pay attention.

Forward

— Liang

Looking around me,

The sky is so bleak,

The air is so calm,

All the scenery

Lacks vitality.

×××

I heard that over there,

Spring has come,

The path of roses,

Is covered with fragrant buds,

This is indeed a lovely environment.

×××

Just as I was about to set off,

I saw a path full of thorns in front of me;

Looking into the distance,

A wide chasm,

With green blood filling the middle,

A line of ramparts,

With white bones scattered around:

This is obviously the sacrifice of the pioneers, how can it not make me timid and frightened!

×××

Just as I was hesitating like this,

And circling around like this,

Suddenly a surge of hot blood,

Rushed to my heart,

Making my fate,

Clear:

Retreat,

And sink into oblivion with the masses,

Stand still,

And be devoured by wolves,

Only by moving forward,

Is there a possibility of reaching the destination.

×××

Forward! Forward!

I am ready to fight with my hot blood,

Even if I follow in the footsteps of my predecessors,

It is still more glorious than not advancing or retreating,

Moreover, my soul,

Is already close to this blissful paradise.

Returning Home

— Ling Mo

I remember the first time I returned to my hometown, it was in mid-February of the lunar calendar, very close to the Qingming Festival. At that time, the weather in Guangdong was getting warmer day by day, and people were wearing thin clothes in light colors, fluttering and carefree, enjoying the pleasant spring sunshine early. My purpose in going back was first for some personal matters, and second because I grew up in other places and had never seen the clansmen at home. Also, my father wanted me to take the opportunity of the Qingming Festival to pay respects at the graves of our grandparents, whom we had never met, as a way of representing him in fulfilling his filial piety. Because of livelihood issues, he had been wandering outside for more than thirty years and never had time to go back and see them, although he was always thinking about them and dreaming about them.

My family is a declining scholarly family. Our ancestors left behind dozens of acres of fields, several farms, and a reputable and well-established money shop. However, the children relied solely on these assets for their livelihood and did nothing. Some were idle, and the so-called mahjong, pai gow, and fan-tan were their daily lives. Some smoked opium, lying in bed, holding their pipes, and puffing clouds of smoke all day long, not knowing what was called the September 18th Incident or the January 28th Incident. When there was no rice or firewood at home, they would say:

"Go to the money shop to withdraw it and charge it to my account."

Days passed. Finally, in this recession year, they went bankrupt. The money shop closed down, owing more than 100,000 silver dollars in debt. The field deeds were either pawned or sold, leaving very little.

Although they saw the ancestral property gradually being sold off and used up, they were still unwilling to be frugal for this Qingming Festival. It seemed that they would rather see the living descendants starve than not have several decent roast pigs to carry up the mountain to sacrifice to these dead ancestors. Not only roast pigs, but also wine, dishes, pastries, and fruits were required. After the grave sweeping ceremony was over, these things would be moved to the ancestral hall and distributed according to the number of descendants in each branch. The wine and dishes would be left until the evening to invite some relatives and friends to eat and drink in the ancestral hall. In fact, they did not sincerely want so many sacrificial offerings to be placed in front of the ancestors' graves; it was just that these people in charge wanted to take this opportunity to skim some money from the public funds, and those who sat idle were happy to not have to spend money, fattening their mouths, and even receiving a share of what was called "sacrificial meat money." They! The men were extremely happy. As for us women? Aren't we also descendants of this family's ancestors? We simply didn't have a share of anything; we were even mocked! And looked down upon!

I was always unhappy to see them treat us women like this, and I stood aside with a sullen face watching them distribute the things. My grand-uncle saw me standing still, and he casually took a share of the sacrificial meat money and gave it to me, and said with a slight smile:

"This is your father's share, you can take it for him."

Just then, our aunt happened to be standing next to me, and when she saw this, she sighed and said to me:

"Why aren't you a boy! Alas, you don't have any brothers, otherwise, you might get several shares today, who knows!" She sighed again, as if she was very worried about her deceased father: because our father – her younger brother – was the eldest son of our grandfather. Their traditional thinking was: only the eldest son can inherit the incense of this family, and no one else can. Therefore, the eldest sons must have an eldest grandson and an eldest daughter-in-law to pass down generation after generation. Coincidentally, our father had only daughters, none of whom suited their tastes. Therefore, they, the brothers and sisters, were very anxious for this branch of the family, and said that our father had to quickly take a concubine and have a son. At the time, I received the money and heard these words, and I felt very uncomfortable. I glanced at my aunt and ran straight home.

Finally, one morning, I said goodbye to them and left my hometown.

Disease Q&A – Answer to Mr. Ye Shengfa of Wuhu

According to the symptoms described in your letter, the child is suffering from acute suppurative myositis. The muscles have shortened after suppuration and changes have occurred. Massage and electrical therapy may help to restore it slightly, but complete recovery may be difficult.

Tokyo Municipal Marriage Agency, Japan

— Wu

Since its establishment, the agency has arranged 54 marriages. The Tokyo Municipal Government of Japan, in order to meet urgent social needs, established a marriage agency in April of last year. To date, after more than a year of work, it has achieved remarkable results. So far, 1,316 people have applied to the agency for marriage introductions. The agency has arranged 54 successful marriages. The survey results are as follows:

Applicants' Gender: 504 men, 812 women.

Applicants' Status: Men are mostly government officials, clerks, and salaried employees with monthly incomes ranging from approximately 60 to 150 yuan. Women mostly come from salaried families with monthly incomes of 200 yuan or more.

Applicants' Education: Most men are primary school graduates, followed by middle school graduates. All women are graduates of secondary or higher schools.

The Future of Sexual Love

— Yun

From whatever angle we look at it, under the current social system, human sexual love is just like a commodity in the stock exchange. On the one hand, only a small number of people are enjoying the happiness of sexual love, while on the other hand, a large number of people are struggling in pain in abnormal sexual love lives. Some people cannot afford to support a wife, so they have to take money to the human flesh market to sell unhealthy sexual love lives. Some people are forced by circumstances to sell their bodies to maintain their lives. At the same time, there are a large number of people who cannot get a satisfactory spouse, and even have to embrace "permanent" singleness!

Therefore, from the past to the present, from the perspective of the historical evolution process, the record of sexual love between men and women is now writing an extremely tragic page. On this page, I don't know how many youths, how much wisdom, and how many lives have been buried!

However, the wheels of history will never remain at a certain stage forever, and the progress of history will inevitably destroy this unhealthy sexual love life of mankind. In the future, when the world's science and production technology have reached the highest stage, and all the wealth of society is completely controlled by human beings themselves, then, the sexual love life between the two sexes will of course break away from the shackles of "commodification" and embark on the right track. In addition to doing very short necessary labor work every day, people can use a lot of time to study science, art, and various specialized knowledge to improve the level of human knowledge. At the same time, there are ample opportunities for various physical exercises and games, as well as attention to all hygiene that is beneficial to the body. In addition, there is a lot of spare time that can be used in various entertainment aspects (such as music, dance, movies, drama, literature...). Under these conditions, the relationship between men and women, the life of sexual love, is not only free from all laws, religions, morality, and rituals, and the restrictions of money, but is purely based on the love of both men and women. Secondly, things like the convergence of thoughts and interests, the common feelings of hobbies and art, and the harmony of physique, appearance, and temperament are also incidental conditions for achieving a perfect love. As for the health of both sexes and all knowledge of sex, at that time, there must be specialized hospitals and health institutions responsible for checking the bodies of men and women, so that those who suffer from syphilis, gonorrhea, tuberculosis, and other infectious diseases are prohibited from marrying, so as not to harm others and the race. And, the absolute freedom of marriage and divorce, as well as the widespread knowledge of proper sex life, will make human sexual love life healthier and more fulfilling!

This is of course not only an ideal, but also an inevitable fact. However, we know that the realization of this fact is by no means just a "fateful" inevitability. The main thing is that we need our arduous and great efforts - because this is by no means a simple problem, this is one department of the entire social problem. To solve this problem, we mainly need the improvement of the entire society.

Concerning News about the New American Cotton Crop

New York, June 8th telegraphs a report on the week's cotton market: Continued rain in the eastern cotton belt and drought in the wheat belt, which may extend to the Southwest, has led to concerns about the future of the cotton crop, triggering speculative demand in the raw cotton market. There are fewer sellers, and market prices are rising. When the July contract price rose to 1.2 cents, short selling increased. There is also news that one-cent loans of cotton are now being gradually transported from the interior. However, talk of inflation has resurfaced, and reports of unfavorable weather continue to circulate, so short selling and profit-taking at slight declines are absorbed by buyers. The East has repeatedly complained of grassy cotton fields and waterlogged cotton stalks. The situation has not yet escalated, but Texas and Oklahoma now need rain. However, if the East continues to experience prolonged rain, it will lead to a major pest infestation, and waterlogged cotton stalks will quickly deteriorate in dry and hot weather. The current labor unrest in the steel industry is concerning and is limiting buying interest in the cotton market.

Many Silkworm Farmers in Jiashan Bake Cocoons Themselves. Cocoon markets in the four townships have been open for over a week, with the highest price for improved breeds at 30 yuan and the price for native breeds at 18 yuan. Farmers cannot cover their leaf costs, so many are drying their own cocoons. Fewer goods are arriving on the market, and the cocoon market will soon end.

Jiangyin Superior Cocoons are Expected to Rise in Price. New cocoons from Jiangyin's four townships are gradually entering the market. There are over thirty cocoon firms open. This year, the price of mulberry leaves is high, and farmers' silkworm costs are higher. However, the price offered by cocoon firms is only 30 yuan for improved breeds and 20 yuan for native breeds. Silkworm farmers are losing money and reluctant to sell. Later, the price rose to 35 yuan, and the price for native breeds was 22 yuan. However, the price of cocoons in neighboring counties (Wujin and Wuxi) is higher, so superior cocoons are expected to rise to 40 yuan.

Shen Bao Amateur Weekly

Amateur Talk

The Collapse of the League of Nations

— A Contribution from Yun Congjun

The result of the First World War, besides the sacrifice of millions of lives and the expenditure of hundreds of billions of dollars, the only achievement was the establishment of an organization to promote world peace – the League of Nations.

When the Treaty of Versailles came into effect on January 10, 1920, and the League of Nations was formally established, politicians and the people suffering from the war around the world celebrated the establishment of this world peace organization with cheers. Everyone believed that the world would be peaceful from then on, and that international peace had been deeply guaranteed.

However, only a little over a decade has passed, and all objective events have proven the error of people's ideals at that time. Although Geneva is still playing peaceful music, what we hear now is the sinister laughter of the god of war. The failure of the disarmament conference, the frantic arms race among the great powers, the Anglo-American hegemony in the world market, the Japanese-American conflict in the Pacific, the intensification of German-French contradictions, and the Russo-Japanese preparations for war in the Far East – all of this is enough to prove that the whole world is now just like the eve of the First World War, with the air everywhere filled with war. Now, except for three-year-old children, probably no one would doubt the inevitable outbreak of a second world war!

In the face of this crisis of a great war, the League of Nations has lost its effectiveness, and the touchstone of all justice, reason, and peace has proven that the League of Nations is just a decaying corpse. In the past, although the League of Nations was an [obscured text] organization of the great powers, it could sometimes be used to ease conflicts between them, or to whitewash world peace. However, now, in the face of the accelerated development of the inherent conflicts of world imperialism, this agency for whitewashing peace cannot but tend towards collapse.

First, Japan tore up international conventions, occupied the three eastern provinces of our country, and formally withdrew from the League of Nations. Then, Germany expressed dissatisfaction with the disarmament issue and formally announced its withdrawal on October 14 last year. Now, although the League of Nations barely exists, the main countries such as the United States, Russia, Japan, and Germany have not participated, and the role of the League of Nations itself has been greatly weakened. In particular, the recent disarmament conference – the only work of the League of Nations – has declared bankruptcy, and the work of the League of Nations has suffered the final test.

Not only that, but even within the current fragmented League of Nations, the imperialist powers are still fighting each other, using it as a center.

In order to seize France's hegemony in Europe, Italy has established the Italian-Austrian-Hungarian alliance, and at the same time is loudly advocating the reorganization of the League of Nations, attempting to use this to seize control of the League of Nations in its own hands, in order to weaken France's power in Europe.

In the past, the United States has always indicated that it would not interfere in the affairs of the League of Nations, but in recent years, the development of American financial power in Europe cannot but cause it to actively intervene in all European political issues. The United States is not only competing with Britain in Europe, but also competing with France. The United States always remembers to undermine the anti-American united front in Europe. Therefore, the United States is not only unwilling to maintain the League of Nations, but also wants to promote its collapse in all aspects.

Those who want to maintain the League of Nations are only France and Britain. Recently, in order to maintain the existence of the League of Nations, Britain and France have tried their best to win over the Soviet Union to join. As for the Soviet Union, it may join the League of Nations in the future in order to consolidate the current Franco-Russian alliance and to deal with fascist Germany, or it may not join the League of Nations after all because the Soviet Union does not want to participate in the vortex of European politics. However, under the current circumstances, the League of Nations is already in a state of fragmentation and disintegration. Even if the Soviet Union joins in the future, it will still be unable to save the crisis of the League of Nations itself!

Under such circumstances, we can see that the fate of the League of Nations has reached the final stage of bankruptcy. The world is a powerful powder keg, and the bankruptcy of the League of Nations shows that the period of peace between the First and Second World Wars has ended, and the gunfire of the Second World War will become the final funeral of the League of Nations!

Four hundred million compatriots on this world battlefield, how shall we cope with all the future events? The League of Nations has collapsed. Do we still have to rely on the League of Nations?

Life

Locusts

— Si Yu

The rural villages in summer are silent under the thick, sultry air. Women, having finished a busy season in the silkworm fields, drag their tired bodies around the houses tidying away all the tools used during silkworm rearing, and also the dried-up silkworm cocoons left over from selling to the cocoon merchants. The men, carrying ploughs and hoes, driving water buffaloes, holding in their hearts the disappointment that this year’s cocoons are also not worth much money, are on their way to the fields, depositing their stomachs full of displeasure on the hoe edges and plough tips, heavily tilling the soil, hoping, hoping that a bountiful autumn harvest will alleviate the pressures of life. The rural villages in summer are silent under the thick, sultry air, and there is little sound of footsteps walking around the villages, even the yellow dogs are dozing under the willow shade or beside the bamboo fence.

Only Sixth Grandpa, the village elder who is respected in Shangxing Village where everyone is busy in the fourth month, is fortunate enough to go to town to sit in a teahouse, drink a bowl of tea, listen to some news from the newspapers that is in reality already old, and then return in the evening crow-call, taking advantage of the fact that the farmers mostly wash their feet, holding bowls and gathering in the open space to eat dinner, and telling everyone stories like Shan Hai Jing (Classic of Mountains and Seas). When the simple listeners find it funny, they will spit grains of rice all over the ground, and then regretfully and fondly bend down to pick them up, blow off the dust and put them back into their mouths, and when they hear something infuriating, they will stomp their ankles and curse the county magistrate “at sea.” Only when they hear that donations are going to be increased again or money and grain are being urged to be paid, each person scatters home with an expression of not knowing whether to laugh or cry, finds faults with his wife or children to scold and beat, using this to vent his anger.

Today, the appearance is a bit different. Shangxing Village, which is usually quiet because everyone is busy working, became agitated after Village Head Sixth Grandpa hurriedly returned early from town. Gui Sheng and his son, who were hoeing in the fields in the west of the village, were the first to see Sixth Grandpa bowing to each field of wheat that was nodding in the wind, muttering something in his mouth. Gui Sheng and his son were a little afraid to interrupt him, so they just stopped hoeing and watched. Sixth Grandpa ordered the two of them to quickly call all the men to carry their hoes home, and then ran rickety to the village.

When the men inexplicably returned to the village, they saw Sixth Grandpa burning incense and lighting candles in front of the Meng Jiang Temple in the east of the village, and they understood half of it, and consciously rushed over with hurried steps, asking Sixth Grandpa if the locusts were coming.

"Locusts, heavens, heavenly insects are coming! They flew over from × County, opened their mouths in the west of the town, and ate all the wheat ears and rice sprouts. Heaven's will, quickly pray to the Bodhisattvas!" Most of the men followed Sixth Grandpa and knelt down, only a few young people hesitated.

The women also ran out from the main rooms, standing not far from the Meng Jiang Temple, looking at this small temple, looking at their husbands or sons kneeling in front of the temple, and then turned their heads worriedly to look at the western sky. The children hid in fear beside their grandmothers or mothers, waiting for the arrival of a great or small misfortune.

Finally, before half a section of incense had been burned, it was the women's shouts that first raised the heads of the kneeling men. Swarms of locusts flew over from the western sky like snowflakes, landing on the threshing ground, in the fields, jumping, jumping wildly everywhere. Disaster has come. The women cried, "Heavens, Bodhisattvas!" The children wailed along. The men, turning pale with anxiety, grabbed the iron and copper gongs that could be banged to make noise and ran to the fields, first running to the wheat fields and paddies, only to see locusts all over the ridges and furrows, but they had not yet used their sharp, scissor-like mouths to bite the wheat ears, but were just tired, as if recuperating. "Bodhisattvas protect us, Meng Jiang has sealed the mouths of the insects, they won't open their mouths, and will save the lives of us people!" Everyone thought so in their hearts, expanding the power of the gods to the highest degree.

Page 20

Sixth Grandpa knelt for a long time in front of the Meng Jiang Temple, vowing: "If their mouths don't open, we will hire a troupe to perform a play to thank the gods, and consecrate the temple!" Before he could finish speaking, the sound of copper gongs and iron instruments, people crying and shouting, and the sky falling, sounded throughout the fields and nearby villages. The locusts flew in the sky like a torrential rain, biting like silkworms eating mulberry leaves in the wheat fields. In an instant, some of the wheat stalks that were half a man tall were broken at the roots and fell down, and some had their ears broken off and hanging. The tender seedlings, only three inches tall, were gnawed leaving only the roots. It's over!

Sixth Grandpa's vow to pray to the gods could not stop the mouths of the locusts, and the copper and iron instruments that everyone was banging could not scare away the swarm of locusts. Only Gui Sheng and his son fought the locusts with brooms, beating half a ditch of locusts to death and preserving more than one mu of rice fields. But in the locust plague where "locust nymphs leave no green grass," it is not yet known whether these surviving rice fields can be preserved.

From then on, Shangxing and the surrounding villages fell into a state after a death attack, and the area of this state extended with the locusts flying and jumping wildly.

The Issue of Reducing Rent

— Ji Chong

The rent reduction movement, which seemed to have subsided on the surface, has once again attracted the attention of the general public due to the conversations between the parties involved in the municipal council's convocation movement, the publication of specific opinions by the Real Estate Association and the Rent Reduction Promotion Association, and the petition submitted by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to the municipal government requesting the formulation of rent reduction measures. Because I feel that this issue is important, I am offering a few opinions here to the general readers, hoping that this will further arouse everyone's attention to the issue, and then try to solve this problem.

×××××

In the past six or seven years, the collapse of the rural economy and the decline of industry and commerce in various places have resulted in a large amount of cash flowing into Shanghai from the interior. According to statistics, in recent years, the amount of cash flowing into Shanghai from the countryside has been as high as 500 to 600 million yuan. However, Shanghai's industry and commerce have also been declining in recent years, and everyone is unwilling to invest in general industry and commerce. Therefore, such a large amount of cash flowing into Shanghai from the interior, as well as the capital originally existing in Shanghai, in addition to being used for securities investment and all kinds of speculative activities, most of it is invested in real estate and in the construction of houses. The Shanghai Real Estate Association stated in its written opinion to the Municipal Council on the issue of rent reduction: "In the past eight years, newly built buildings were worth about 500 million yuan, and adding the old buildings, it should be around 2 billion yuan." This is clear evidence of the development of the construction industry in Shanghai in recent years.

At the same time, the collapse of the rural economy and the unrest in inland society have caused a large population to flow to Shanghai. Therefore, although the number of houses in Shanghai has increased greatly in recent years, rents have not decreased at all, but have increased a lot. In the past six or seven years, the standard index of 260 kinds of daily necessities in Shanghai has fallen by 20%, while rents have increased by 12%. This further explains why people are willing to invest in real estate rather than in industry and commerce.

However, the decline of general industry and commerce will inevitably lead to the bankruptcy, unemployment, and impoverishment of a large number of people, and even make it difficult for them to eat and live in houses. Even the Real Estate Association knows: "Recently, factories in the eastern district have declined, commerce in the central district is particularly depressed, and the northern district has not yet recovered from its wounds. Only the western district has expanded greatly, and residents have difficulty making a living, often moving from large houses to small houses, and renting out houses by dividing them. Thus, the general public cannot continue to bear this excessive rent, and the issue of rent reduction has arisen, and the rent reduction movement has expanded day by day. According to the "Shen Bao" on February 20, there are already more than a dozen countries participating in the rent reduction movement, and among foreigners, Japanese, Russians and Indians are the most numerous.

The occurrence and expansion of the rent reduction movement is not only displeasing to those who manage real estate, but also makes the giants of the financial world very unhappy. Because the latter, in addition to managing their own real estate, also accept mortgages on other people's real estate. If rents are really reduced, the huge profits they make in managing real estate and in mortgage loans will inevitably be reduced by a lot. Therefore, as soon as the rent reduction issue was raised, they expressed their opposition. They said that the real estate market has been declining recently, and once rents are reduced, the huge capital invested in real estate will inevitably be affected; the result will not only affect finance, but also hinder the prosperity of the market, and the impact on society will be not shallow. However, on the other hand, in the midst of this economic downturn and difficult livelihood, the general industrialists, merchants and most of the citizens are unable to continue to bear the excessive rent; if such high rents as they are now cannot be reduced, then bankruptcy, unemployment and other phenomena will inevitably become more widespread and profound. In this way, the two sides are at loggerheads, and the problem has not been resolved until now.

In my opinion, the owners of houses in Shanghai are not only the giants of the Chinese financial world, but also foreign rich men, and they all have the greatest authority in Shanghai. Even the Municipal Chamber of Commerce recently stated in its petition to the municipal government that it "is limited by the power of capital" and "dare not lightly agree" to the rent reduction movement. Under these circumstances, if the general public does not make greater efforts, it is afraid that it will be very problematic to want the rent reduction movement to have good results.

However, in any case, a large number of industrialists and merchants are closing down because they cannot afford the excessive rent, and a large number of people are being driven to shacks and even the streets because they cannot pay the excessive rent: these phenomena are always very serious. The impact of this serious phenomenon on market prosperity and social order must be much greater than the loss of a little profit by a few real estate owners. Therefore, I hope that the municipal authorities can pay special attention to it and fairly resolve this issue of rent reduction; naturally, the general public also needs to make greater efforts to realize their hopes.

In the Laboratory

— Xue Wen

I remember four years ago, I came from a university in the interior to this society. Because my "academic" performance was good (the "knowledge" of a university student is naturally limited), I was grateful to the president of the university for hiring me as a teaching assistant in the Department of Sociology of the Faculty of Arts. The career problem that every young person who comes out of university faces was easily solved in this way, and I couldn't help but rejoice in my heart; but after starting work, I found that I should be more worried than happy.

The first thing that bothers people is their own lack of academic ability. I only peddled a little superficial knowledge in college, and I didn’t even fully acquire tool knowledge like English, which inevitably caused obstacles in my work, and therefore I couldn’t make the expected progress in my research work.

Secondly, the heavy burden of complicated work will prevent you from having any ease and leisure in your mind. You have to get to the laboratory at eight o'clock in the morning and work there until twelve o'clock: after a lunch break, you work from one o'clock to five o'clock. You have to work eight hours a day like this, and only the weekly holiday is your own day.

This kind of laboratory life should be welcomed by every person who studies. But the person who said this did not really understand the content of laboratory life. The "chores" inside are more than the "research". This kind of teaching assistant is also a librarian, draftsman, custodian, secretary, general affairs, etc. at the same time, and these jobs are exceptionally mechanical and exceptionally dull.

For example, the work of grading papers and marking scores is definitely not welcome. Our director teaches two sociology courses, each class has one hundred and thirty to forty people, totaling two hundred and sixty to seventy papers. He has to give an exam every three or four weeks. Often, the first batch of exam papers has just been returned, and the second batch is coming again. These exam questions have to be prepared by you. Ordinary essay questions are not important because there are few questions. Once you encounter test questions, you have to find one hundred questions in the not-so-many teaching materials, which is really not easy. Collecting and organizing materials is also a mechanical and complicated task. We are willing to read newspapers, but we are not willing to cut out and paste useful materials from newspapers, even though we know that this is beneficial. After pasting, we also need to classify and organize according to their nature for reference and inspection. Every day, we have to spend more than three hours on three or four kinds of Chinese and Western newspapers.

Drawing is also an important and complicated research work. During my year as a teaching assistant, I drew many pictures about anthropology, demography, social investigation and special research. Each picture takes at least eight or nine hours, and difficult pictures take three to five days of your time. There is a map of the distribution density of population around the world, I remember I spent almost four days on it.

There are also some "special researches" that require you to spend a lot of time. For example, the investigation and statistics of family problems and marriage problems, the analysis of famous people in various dynasties and the distribution of geography in research, the local practical investigation of urban society and rural society, and problems such as suicide, crime, and unemployment all require you to share a part of your energy. Although students are responsible for these topics, you have to assist them in the position of a mentor, and you must also study a topic alone, otherwise you will have no performance in research, and the tragedy of the result is not difficult to imagine.

There are also nearly 30 kinds of Chinese and English sociology publications and 200 to 300 sociology books in the laboratory, and the responsibility of managing these undoubtedly falls on you. When each new book is reported, you have to register it on the card, and when you lend it out, you have to go through all the borrowing procedures for books and newspapers with the students.

Also, during the exam, you have to issue papers and invigilate. This has a difficulty, some of these students are your friends, or friends of your friends; not long ago we were all "classmates", now can I put on a straight face in front of them and interfere with them cheating? If you are really so "arrogant", you may encounter indecision. So in this case, you have to pretend to be careless, as if you are blind, and have not seen them doing things that damage their personality. Grading the papers has the same difficulty as this. For example, the papers are only worth fifty-seven or eight points, you can't help but give them a passing grade.

The kind of life mentioned above will inevitably make people feel mentally tired and thirsty for rest. Sleep is sweet in such a situation, and this was not experienced in college days.

The reward for such hard work is 60 yuan per month. This is neither too much nor too little. I heard that a teaching assistant at a certain university in Shanghai only has 30 yuan a month. There must be a reason why a college student who has spent two or three thousand yuan (calculated for four years, at least 500 yuan per year) is willing to sell knowledge labor at such a low price: one is that it is not easy to find a job, and the other is to obtain a good qualification (a qualification second only to that of a professor). It's good to go to the interior and sell it at a high price. This is the situation in private universities. Teaching assistants in national or provincial universities receive 80 to 100 yuan per month. If you can teach some classes in high school, the income will be even more considerable. However, this kind of luck is not common, unless you have a special relationship with the school authorities.

Outport Postal Agency

Titled The Fragrant Smoke of Miaofeng Mountain

— Bi Mei

Beiping Correspondence

Miaofeng Mountain is located in the northwest of Beiping. It is said that the Holy Mother of Miaofeng Mountain is very efficacious, so every year, the pious men and women who go to the mountain to offer incense are very crowded.

On the first day of the fourth lunar month this year, the temple gate was wide open. Because the situation was unstable last year, many people did not offer incense, so this year's incense is more prosperous than in previous years. What is even more different from previous years is that foreigners from the East and the West also followed our country's pious men and women to the mountain to offer incense. There were quite a few of them. When the pious men and women of Europe went down the mountain, they also wrapped their heads in yellow cloth towels and inserted velvet flowers. Beiping calls this "returning home with a blessing", and I think these foreign men and women also have this kind of thinking?

Miaofeng Mountain is so high, so the top of the mountain is often covered with snow. People who go to offer incense must bring cotton clothes with them, because the top of the mountain is so cold, it is like another world compared to the foot of the mountain.

Here, there is no distinction between the rich and the poor. All that is seen are the old, the young, the men and the women, all busily going up the mountain to offer incense. Some are repaying vows for the illnesses of their parents, husbands, wives, and children, taking one step and kowtowing once, taking three steps and kowtowing once. The mountain is so high that it takes several days to reach the temple at the top of the mountain. The rich can go up by sedan chair, and the poor can only use their feet as a car. Those who walk slowly can reach it in one or two days.

There are small shops beside the mountain where you can stay overnight, and there are small food stalls where you can buy food to fill your stomach. What is strange is that money is not a concern. The rich can give more, and the poor give less. They don’t argue about it.

It is said that you have to say good things when you go up the mountain. If your heart is not sincere, you will not be able to reach the top of the mountain. Even if you try your best to climb up, you will fall down. Also, you cannot say: "Oh! My shoes are going to break!" Then your shoes will really break and you will not be able to go up the mountain. On the contrary, even if your shoes are already broken, but you don't care at all and sincerely want to offer incense, then until you return home after offering incense, the shoes will still be the same as

Living Circle

— Bai Yu

The morning sun, faintly revealing lead-gray cloud cover, golden arrows of light, lifted the gauze of dense fog, dawn, alternating in the breath of darkness.

The silhouette of the city's side. The authority-wielding whistle, shrieking sharply, shattered the bitter dreams of countless laborers buried in life.

Strings of dark black smoke, belched angrily from towering cloud-peaked chimneys, destroying the sweat and blood of exploitation.

On the hunger line, a group of exhausted coolies struggled, their trembling steps, entering the tiger's mouth that dominates life.

The sound of machinery under the rotation of motors, the miserable cries under the lashes of whips, symphonized into the decline of the world.

Hot wind, carrying spiciness, hot wind flying from the equator. But, unable to awaken the universe intoxicated in a pink atmosphere.

Wooden axles, tapping on rough stone roads, cut through the loneliness of the air.

A chaotic dawn road, etched with chaotic human traces, imprinted with a chaotic car shadow.

Morning wind, swirling the dust and sand on the cement, black wooden boxes, burying them.

A dark sauce face, a withered, tattered, dirty hat, red clothes, all symbolizing that he is a street cleaner under the rolling wheels.

The city's garbage, no, the city's sins! Wore away his tiny life.

A lively vigor, permeated the living circle of the early market.

The sound of people, the long neighs of horses, everything, people surviving in a sea of madness.

The disappearance of Little Liu Zi's car, the police caught Eight Hands [a thief], scientific spirit mediums [Ouija boards] were popular all over the streets, bargain sale flags fluttered all year round, everything. A deformed society, revealing its true nature.

In the center of the street, a group of young girls, they sang with affection: Selling flowers! Pearl flowers! White orchid!

Scarlet roses, reflecting scarlet faces, clear singing, stirring the restless hearts of everyone: sad emotions, disappearing with the withered flowers. Swallow-like they are, innocent, beautiful. They do not know that the iron chains of life have already tightly locked their youthful lives, pitiful! They never even imagined that the black shadow of urban sin, has surrounded their entire fragile soul.

Just like when I first came, it won't be too broken.

On the way up the mountain, everyone smiles and nods to each other. There is no hypocrisy, ferocity, no class consciousness here, everyone is as close as a family, helping each other, so the road is not lonely.

The temple on the top of the mountain is very large, and pilgrims can live inside, and vegetarian dishes are served every day to feed the pious men and women. Because of the divine efficacy of the Holy Mother of Miaofeng, everyone is happy to obtain a divination slip. It is said that the divination slips of the Holy Mother of Miaofeng are also very efficacious! (?)

In this era, there are the most people who believe in Buddha, and everyone seeks the blessing and help of the old Buddha in everything. On the way from Beiping to Miaofeng Mountain, countless men and women can be seen carrying yellow bundles, wearing yellow scarves around their heads, etc.

The temple is only open once a year, and the mountain gate closes after the tenth day of the fourth month. If you want to offer incense again, you have to wait another year!

The income from incense fees is countless and quite considerable. Generally, people are happy to do good deeds and are willing to donate more money to the Holy Mother of Miaofeng as incense fees, asking her to bless them with peace. But it is not easy to get them to donate to charity.

Even though it is a year of economic bankruptcy and panic is raging everywhere, here, it is still as dignified and luxurious as before, and there is no sign of poverty.

——Store Clerk Training of John Wanamaker Department Store

1. Should possess the character of a gentleman.

7. Speech and behavior should be elegant and lively.

On Suicide

— Ms. Lixing

"Suicide, it is too cowardly and takes life too lightly for good young people to willingly commit suicide, even though the environment is so difficult...!"

This is the current criticism of young people who commit suicide.

Living people criticize the dead in order to encourage the living, because the stakes for humans are more closely related than for other closely related animals, so the impact is also greater. In fact, we are shocked when we hear that someone has committed suicide, especially those of the same class, and it is easier to feel a sense of shared grief. But when we encounter "living dead" (people who waste social wealth, sit and eat without doing anything), we only take it lightly. Fairly speaking, is it better to linger on, endure humiliation and live in shame, since living does not contribute to livelihood, and when you die, you can not only go to the same destination as the wealthy and the rich, return to the realm of death praised in "Keats" "Nightingale Song", where everything disharmonious is harmonious, but also, debts owed to others absolutely do not need to be repaid, which is considered to have reached the realm of equal freedom in spirit, which is much better than living in anger? This is an experimental view of life.

Some people absolutely refuse to commit suicide. These people are always casual in their work and get by in life. When evaluating people and things, they always use the spirit of a female antelope observing the wind and smelling enemies to respond, and they never dare to have their own opinions, so the conclusion is nothing more than yes! yes! The souls of these people are similar to the flying catkins in the spring suburbs, fluttering. Their way of survival is the same as that of horses and cattle, working hard all day long without knowing why, this is a view of life.

Some people look down on suicide and ridicule suicide. These people have a gloomy view of life, do not know about public welfare, and are not confused by spiritual creation. They believe in the philosophy that "justice is the interest of the strong, good people are ignorant, and the important thing is to be wise", and use their life's energy to create personal happiness. If you ask this kind of person what is the meaning of living, he will ask you what is the purpose of human survival. If you think their lives are a waste, they will laugh at your struggle, leaving only a few strands of unsellable hair as a symbol of cowardice. Even if the country is broken and the enemy is approaching, they will never commit suicide or resist out of indignation; because they have long been prepared to go abroad to be world-weary slaves of a fallen country.

There are also some people who express sympathy for those who commit suicide, but they themselves will never commit suicide. Most of these people are strong-willed. They sometimes fall into difficult living conditions, but they are not pessimistic because of this. They express great sympathy for the oppressed, take the suffering of most people as their own suffering, and take the shame of the country and the nation as their own shame; they are actually complete fools, and they suffer more setbacks than ordinary people, but they often enjoy less material pleasure than ordinary people. However, the spiritual realm of such people occupies a larger area than that of ordinary people, if they succeed in something that is beneficial to the masses.

However, such fools are rarely found in the present society; because there are too many smart people in China now, unless they are willing to fight desperately for their own interests, they are almost surprised when they hear the behavior of the above-mentioned fools; therefore, Chinese people may have the same fate as Jews in the future.

In this society with too many smart people, the number of people who die by suicide is increasing day by day, and at the same time, there are more people living in slow suicide; it is just that the former is obvious, but the latter has already stepped onto the former's path while laughing at the former, but they are still not aware of it until death.

International Broadcasting Radio Station

The Apprentice School Founded by American Entrepreneur Ford

— Chen Jiyun

The apprenticeship system is indeed a very good system, but in our China, there is only dead work, day and night without rest time, like hard labor, which has a great impact on all aspects of underage children, poor development, and the rampage of tuberculosis. It can be said that all these are the result of this kind of life. Now I will introduce the apprentice school run by the American entrepreneur Ford below for the reference of the industrial and commercial circles:

The original purpose of Ford's Apprentice School was to only accept orphans who had no guardians or parents, so that they would have the opportunity to work in the future. Later, the children of Ford employees could also enroll at will. This school of his is to train workers, and its purpose is to create people who can manage their own lives. Not only does he want them to be able to be self-reliant, but also to make them more able to manage a good life than others, but giving them the privilege of working is not to cultivate their dependence, but to cultivate their ability to create and control their own lives. Therefore, according to this method, his school's educational policy

, there are three important points. First, boys are still boys. Don't make them early successful activists. Second, academic studies should go hand in hand with experimentation. Third, it is not divorced from reality education, and his products must be practical and useful. Let's look at his detailed implementation of this article below.

(1) Children should naturally be treated like children, and children's nature should be encouraged. Observing children in factories and classrooms is to make them see their own light, to make them have the consciousness of being their own "masters", to make them know that they are doing things for themselves, to make them feel interested and necessary to be enthusiastic, to make them want to learn what children should learn, and to learn the questions that they want to ask at home but no one answers them.

Even if children want to be workers, they must not forget that they are children. This point is the most important. After their products are inspected, they are sold to Ford Motor Company as funding for the school. If there are bad products, it will be a loss to the school. Therefore, students and schools must cheer up and work hard, and unknowingly, they have developed a sense of responsibility for doing things. Therefore, the school's factory also gives them bonuses ranging from seven yuan and two cents to eighteen yuan a week. After they graduate, they will not only have a general education, but also have considerable professional knowledge. Their skills are as skilled as adults, so they can go to any factory to do things. If they are willing to continue their studies, they can also work part-time and study part-time with considerable proficiency, and get higher wages. There is no regulation that they must work in the Ford factory after graduation.

(2) Knowledge and technology cannot advance at the same time. This is the second principle. Dead knowledge and book knowledge are not the knowledge of workers. It must be living knowledge and practical knowledge. Naturally, technology cannot be obtained by relying solely on prototype practice. Therefore, their textbooks are the Ford factory. For example, the arithmetic taught is a practical and useful problem in the actual activities of the factory.

Geography is also the same. It asks: What ship should you take to send a car to Singapore? Which way to go? Even the list receipts are shown to them. This is how it is pushed to all parts of the world, and the real commercial routes are explained to them in detail one by one. The physics and chemistry taught are also the same. The teachers explain from the actual situation, and the students also ask from the actual situation, disassembling the machines one by one to explain, and then teaching them how to install them so that they can turn. If students want to make noble and subtle products, they must understand the corresponding difficult problems, and they must also explain them in detail. And they often have to learn to repair machines.

(3) It is not allowed to hurt the self-esteem of students, the self-esteem of producing goods by their own activities, to help increase their sense of responsibility, this is the third concept. Therefore, they must work at school, and they are also paid for their work. At the Ford School, at the beginning, one-third of the day was spent teaching in the classroom, and two-thirds of the day was spent teaching work in the factory. Later, I learned that changing like this in one day greatly hindered their progress. Now it is stipulated that they will teach in the classroom for one week and teach work in the factory for two weeks.

In addition to the above-mentioned academic courses and internships, there are also games and gymnastics, which are the same as ordinary schools. On Fridays, there are also many meetings in the purchasing hall, where they can freely discuss.

The facilities of the Ford Apprentice School are like this. I wonder how the agencies in China that implement the apprenticeship system will feel after reading it.
