Commentary

On Promoting Physical Education

— Shao Wen

In recent years, our old China seems to be talking about being modern. Advocating something, reviving something, has become our most modern slogan. If everyone really "works hard" and "works hard" according to these modern slogans, then the old China may become an American-style modern country. However, unfortunately, when we advocate domestic products, those modern girls and young masters specialize in buying foreign goods; when we work hard to revive the rural movement, those rich masters and wives insist on depositing their gold and silver treasures in foreign banks instead of taking them to the rural areas to circulate. As a result, the movement to promote domestic products failed: as a result, rural finance was in trouble, and the entire movement to revive rural areas achieved no results.

However, things cannot always be generalized. Although we have failed in other movements and have no achievements, we have gained a lot in promoting physical education. Look, how lively are the local sports meets, the national sports meets, and the Far Eastern Games! Every time these sports meets are held, large and small newspapers across the country have to publicize and promote them with the largest amount of space; today, a certain female wolf is published in the place where she is powerful, and tomorrow, a certain soldier wins the championship alone. The tension of the situation is no less than the arrival of World War II! 丨丨 From this, we can see how enthusiastic and unified people are about promoting physical education, and how great achievements our movement to promote physical education has shown!

However, I don't know what the meaning of promoting physical education in this way is. I think that physical education can only be regarded as a part of our daily homework and should not be regarded as the only important task. If young people always run, jump, swim, play ball, and engage in physical education, regardless of everything, what kind of people will they become as a result? What contributions will they make to the country, society, academic, and culture besides being able to run and jump? This is not difficult to imagine. At the same time, the purpose of physical education should be to strengthen the body, not to compete for victory and show off like gambling. However, the physical education we are promoting now is promoting it as a specialized career. The students of various physical education schools, all athletes, in addition to exercising all day long, not only do not ask about all issues related to the country and society, but even do not study various academic subjects. Look, aren't nine out of ten athletes simple-minded and uneducated? As for the purpose of their exercising all day long, it is of course to want to be athletes, go to sports meets, and win championships. 丨丨 Promoting physical education like this is obviously for other purposes.

Some people say that promoting physical education can save the country. If the people of the whole country become strong due to the promotion of physical education, wouldn't the country become strong? That's right, if the country wants to be strong, the people must be healthy. If the people are all weak and sick, the country will not be strong, but it cannot be said that as long as the people have healthy bodies, the country will be rich and strong. The natives of Africa, the blacks of America, and the Indian Asans are all very strong, but they don't even have a country now. At the same time, the health of the people's bodies cannot be obtained by promoting physical education in this way. We know that people who have no food to eat, no clothes to wear, and suffer from hunger and cold, pain and sorrow, will never be healthy no matter what. At present, most of the Chinese people are unemployed, poor, hungry, and under the attack of cold. Under this situation, it is a dream to try to promote physical education in this way to strengthen the bodies of the people and thus save the country from danger?

In fact, all the disasters in China are directly or indirectly caused by imperialism. To revitalize China, there is no need to promote physical education in this way, but we need to lead the Chinese people to rise up and fight against imperialism with correct methods. I dare to assert that if the Chinese people all rise up to save the country, China can immediately get rid of all disasters! On the contrary, if we want the general public to ignore all issues related to the country and society and only promote gambling-like physical education, the result will be that even if we win all the championships in the global sports meet, the danger of the country will not be eliminated because of this.

"Winning glory for the country" is what people often use to encourage the "athletes" who go abroad to participate in sports meets. Its meaning is: Although everything is inferior to others, if our "athletes" win in some sports meet abroad, then the country will be very glorious. Therefore, we should promote physical education to "win glory for the country". This is completely an expression of Ah Qism! The land of the country has been taken away province by province, and the people of the whole country are suffering from the bullying and oppression of imperialism. Instead of trying to reform ourselves, we want to promote physical education to "win glory for the country". Apart from the Ah Q Mr. who is good at deceiving and comforting himself, I am afraid no one can do it.

Moreover, to be honest, if we are always so backward and the country always maintains this state, then we will not be able to win any "glory" in any global sports meet or Far Eastern Games. The fact that the Far Eastern Games were manipulated by Japan this time is a clear example.

Amateur Study

Mobile Bookstore

— Shaqi

Following the start of the second five-year plan, in every "collective farm" and farmer dormitory in the Soviet countryside, during the spring plowing and sowing and the autumn harvest and distribution of grain seasons, large numbers of motorcycle trucks loaded with various books suitable for farmers to read came to sell to farmers at extremely low prices. Each truck is a bookstore, and they call these motorcycles "mobile bookstores". In addition to selling books, they also come with film projectors and radios, showing and broadcasting the best programs for free, so that ordinary farmers can receive good education while being entertained.

"Mobile Bookstores" are organized directly by the "Central Book Society" of the People's Culture and Education Committee of the Central Soviet. The "Central Book Society" sets up a Turkish-style kiosk in each "political division" in the countryside, which can also be said to be a book station. Each kiosk is equipped with a motorcycle truck loaded with books, etc., and drives around the farms and dormitories.

Before the spring plowing this year (1934), the People's Culture and Education Committee of Moscow mobilized 1,000 members to go to the countryside to participate in their "Central Book Society". One thousand new Turkish-style kiosks were added, three hundred of which were set up in collective farms, specifically for general sowing farmers to purchase, and two hundred were attached to the railway transportation bureau. The "Central Book Society" has now opened 3,520 kiosks, and it is expected that it will increase to 4,500 by the autumn harvest season of this year.

In order to make it easier for ordinary farmers to approach the thoughts of literature and art, the "Central Book Society" implemented the resolution of the People's Culture and Education Committee last year and compiled a catalog of books specifically for the people of the countryside to read. This includes 85 famous literary and artistic works that have been handed over to the National Publishing Department for printing. In order to make it easier for farmers to examine and select the books they love, the "Central Book Society" has specially used the most simple language to make detailed explanations under each catalog. The National Publishing Department also uses large-sized type to print, so that ordinary farmers can read it without any effort.

During the spring plowing this year, the "Central Book Society" transported 100 packages of new books from Moscow to the kiosks in the political divisions of each township every day, and then circulated from there to various collective farms. The readers here have now obtained 6.5 million volumes of literary and artistic books.

The State Retail Industry in the Five-Year Plan

— Li Ren

The rapid growth of the Soviet national economy is accompanied by the development of the state retail trade. The reason for such growth and development is undoubtedly the improvement of the general people's living conditions.

Based on the massive development of heavy industry, the reconstruction of the socialist rural economy, and the increase in commodity production, the development of light industry, whether in terms of production quantity or the reconstruction of the technical base, has become very possible.

The development of light industry is the driving force behind the prosperity of the state retail industry.

In the past eleven years, the trade volume of the Soviet state retail industry was only 3,560,000,000 rubles in 1922/23, but increased to 39,900,000,000 rubles in 1932 (the total for eleven years).

Due to the development of state retail industry and cooperative organizations, private capital trade has been excluded from the market.

In 1922/23, private trade accounted for 75.3 percent of the total national trade; this percentage dropped to 5.8 percent by 1930, and by 1931, this type of private operation had completely lost its position.

The Soviet state retail industry began to develop in 1930, and reached its peak in 1931 and 1932. The trade volume in 1930 was only 2,500,000,000 rubles, rose to 6,500,000,000 rubles in 1931, and increased to 8,000,000,000 rubles in 1932.

The state retail industry is managed by a commercial committee, through large retail stores, and many commercial trusts specializing in selling a certain type of goods. For example, the meat industry trust, under which many stores specialize in selling meat. The milk trust specializes in supplying daily milk. The fish industry trust specializes in supplying the public with various fish foods.

In addition, there are sales organizations specializing in selling a certain type of common daily necessities. For example, many stores of the clothing industry trust specialize in selling clothing. Many stores of the textile trust specialize in selling textiles, and so on.

In addition to these special stores, there are also department stores containing various departments; customers can buy all kinds of goods they want here.

The Soviet planned economy enables more than 300,000 of the above-mentioned various stores to serve the vast public interest in the most suitable and convenient places.

It should also be mentioned that under this state retail system, there is also the establishment of model stores that use modern commercial technology and pay attention to how to serve customers. The organization of common commercial affairs, the precise measurement of goods, the maximum use of mechanical commercial equipment, the application of the "cash on delivery" system, the quick delivery of goods to the buyer's home, etc., these are the characteristics of this model store.

The state retail industry organization also includes many food and beverage stores, such as hotels, cafeterias, kitchen factories, etc., which also serve the vast public interest.

The development of the state retail industry and cooperatives has followed the prosperity of trade in collective farms. Collective farmers and individual small farmers bring their surplus goods to the city and sell them to state commercial organizations at prevailing prices.

According to the provisions of the Second Five-Year Plan, special attention should be paid to specialized trust industries, that is, special attention should be paid to the supply of clothing, shoes and socks, and groceries; the same attention should also be paid to the supply of food raw materials such as butter, fish, and meat, etc.

In addition to these, the Second Five-Year Plan also stipulates that many large department stores should be opened, and many high-rise buildings have now been built for this type of store.

The planned increase of the state retail industry, in the Second Five-Year Plan, pays the same attention to the interests of workers and collective farmers. This enables the planned development of Soviet commerce and commercial technology to become a high-speed leap.

Those who believe they are competent should prepare a letter of resume in English and send it to Mr. Wang Binxian, No. 51 Zhifu Road.

Those who can also take on writing work are especially welcome. Those who wish to apply can send a letter to Zou Zuotong at Shanghai University, Yangshupu.

Scientific Miscellany

Aviation Saves the Nation: The Story of the Invention of the Airship (1)

— Shulin

I. Longing for the Flight of Birds

When we were young, when we saw birds flying freely in the air, we thought in our hearts: "How pleasant it would be if we could fly like that too!"

When the wheat is ripe, walking in the countryside, many swallows turn their white bellies and fly back and forth. When we see it, we hope that we will also become swallows.

Flying in the air is the greatest hope of mankind since the beginning of time. No matter which country's mythology, there must be angels with wings or heavenly horses with flying feathers appearing, flying freely in the air. From this, we can understand how much people in the past longed for flying.

However, until recently, it was absolutely impossible for humans to fly in the air. The famous Wright brothers flew in the air with their own invented airplane in 1903, only twenty or thirty years ago.

Here, we cannot but know: the invention of the airplane took the precious time, money, and even sometimes the loss of their own lives of countless people to succeed.

"The airplane was invented by Wright, it is the result of Wright's painstaking efforts, ——" In fact, it is not as simple as that. Before Wright's invention, there were already countless people who died silently with grievances because they could not achieve their goals.

An invention can never be accomplished by the power of one person. Most people accumulate research, little by little, and once create an invention. Before the invention, who knows how much sacrifice has been paid!

II. The Origin of Balloons

There are various distinctions between machines that fly in the air. Now, let's divide them roughly into two categories:

1. Machines heavier than air

2. Machines lighter than air

Machines heavier than air are the current airplanes. The machine itself is heavier than air and cannot float in the air statically. On the contrary, machines lighter than air are the current airships. The machine itself is lighter than air and can float quietly in the air like a moon floating in the sea. (To be continued)
